## // AxiMinds Neural Computer — axicore Compute Savings Layer
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// The FULL axicore stack available to the AI's neural computer.
// Every optimization the host system gets, the AI's computer gets too.
//
// axicore consolidation architecture:
// Layer 0: axicore (INT1/SPZA/MEP/memoization/SIMD/SMURFS)
// Layer 1: aximodel (model-level abstractions)
// Layer 2: axihw (RKNN2/NEON/CUDA/WASM hardware dispatch)
// Layer 3: axillm (LLM integration)
//
// Compute savings primitives (all available to the neural computer):
// 1. TricacheL1/L2/L3 — Three-tiered cache hierarchy
// 2. INT1 Consensus — 1-bit voting, 3-30 nines of precision
// 3. Shift-Add Everywhere — Zero hardware multiplies in hot paths
// 4. SPZA Memoization — 8D angular-indexed semantic cache
// 5. MEP Routing — Minimum Energy Path for compute dispatch
// 6. SMURFS 4D — θ/φ/ψ/τ at 2^60 scale persona state
// 7. zNorm — Normalization at 2^70 scale
// 8. Hardware Abstraction — NEON/RKNN2/CUDA/scalar auto-dispatch
//
// Zig 0.15.2 | ZLS 0.15.0
const std = @import("std");
const core = @import("types.zig");
const log = std.log.scoped(.axinc_axicore);
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 1. TRICACHE — Three-Tiered Cache Hierarchy
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// Pattern of Threes applied to caching:
// L1: Hot cache — 256 entries, direct-mapped, ~1 cycle access
// L2: Warm cache — 4K entries, 4-way set-associative, ~4 cycle access
// L3: Cold cache — 64K entries, fully-associative LRU, ~16 cycle access
//
// Every compute result flows through this hierarchy. The AI's neural
// computer gets the same tiered caching that axicore uses on the host.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
/// Cache entry: key-value with metadata
pub const CacheEntry = struct {
    key_hash: u64 = 0,
    value: i64 = 0,
    tag: u32 = 0, // operation tag (which ALU op produced this)
    age: u16 = 0, // LRU age counter (L3 only)
    valid: bool = false,
    dirty: bool = false, // modified since last promotion
    pub fn invalidate(self: *CacheEntry) void {
        self.valid = false;
        self.dirty = false;
    }
};
/// L1: Direct-mapped hot cache
/// Smallest, fastest. One entry per hash bucket.
/// Used for: loop-invariant values, constant expressions, repeated MUL results
pub const TricacheL1 = struct {
    pub const SIZE: usize = 256;
    entries: [SIZE]CacheEntry = [*]CacheEntry{.{}} ** SIZE,
    hits: u64 = 0,
    misses: u64 = 0,
    evictions: u64 = 0,
    pub fn lookup(self: *TricacheL1, key_hash: u64) ?i64 {
        const idx = key_hash & (SIZE - 1);
        const entry = &self.entries[idx];
        if (entry.valid and entry.key_hash == key_hash) {
            self.hits += 1;
            return entry.value;
        }
        self.misses += 1;
        return null;
    }
    pub fn store(self: *TricacheL1, key_hash: u64, value: i64, tag: u32) void {
        const idx = key_hash & (SIZE - 1);
        const entry = &self.entries[idx];
        if (entry.valid and entry.key_hash != key_hash) {
            self.evictions += 1;
        }
        entry.* = .{
            .key_hash = key_hash,
            .value = value,
            .tag = tag,
            .valid = true,
        };
    }
    pub fn hitRate(self: *const TricacheL1) f32 {
        const total = self.hits + self.misses;
        if (total == 0) return 0.0;
        return @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.hits)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(total));
    }
};
/// L2: 4-way set-associative warm cache
/// Medium size, medium speed. Catches L1 misses.
/// Used for: function-local temporaries, partial computation results
pub const TricacheL2 = struct {
    pub const SETS: usize = 1024;
    pub const WAYS: usize = 4;
    pub const SIZE: usize = SETS * WAYS;
    entries: [SETS][WAYS]CacheEntry = [*][WAYS]CacheEntry{[*]CacheEntry{.{}} ** WAYS} ** SETS,
    hits: u64 = 0,
    misses: u64 = 0,
    evictions: u64 = 0,
    pub fn lookup(self: *TricacheL2, key_hash: u64) ?i64 {
        const set_idx = key_hash & (SETS - 1);
        const set = &self.entries[set_idx];
        for (set) |*entry| {
            if (entry.valid and entry.key_hash == key_hash) {
                self.hits += 1;
                entry.age = 0; // refresh LRU
                return entry.value;
            }
        }
        self.misses += 1;
        return null;
    }
    pub fn store(self: *TricacheL2, key_hash: u64, value: i64, tag: u32) void {
        const set_idx = key_hash & (SETS - 1);
        const set = &self.entries[set_idx];
        // Find empty way or LRU victim
        var victim_idx: usize = 0;
        var max_age: u16 = 0;
        for (set, 0..) |*entry, i| {
            if (!entry.valid) {
                victim_idx = i;
                break;
            }
            if (entry.age >= max_age) {
                max_age = entry.age;
                victim_idx = i;
            }
        }
        if (set[victim_idx].valid) self.evictions += 1;
        set[victim_idx] = .{
            .key_hash = key_hash,
            .value = value,
            .tag = tag,
            .valid = true,
        };
        // Age all other entries in this set
        for (set, 0..) |*entry, i| {
            if (i != victim_idx and entry.valid) {
                entry.age +|= 1; // saturating increment
            }
        }
    }
    pub fn hitRate(self: *const TricacheL2) f32 {
        const total = self.hits + self.misses;
        if (total == 0) return 0.0;
        return @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.hits)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(total));
    }
};
/// L3: Fully-associative cold cache with LRU eviction
/// Largest, slowest tier. Dynamically allocated.
/// Used for: cross-function results, SPZA spatial lookups, LANG macro results
pub const TricacheL3 = struct {
    pub const DEFAULT_SIZE: usize = 65536;
    entries: []CacheEntry,
    capacity: usize,
    count: usize = 0,
    hits: u64 = 0,
    misses: u64 = 0,
    evictions: u64 = 0,
    global_age: u16 = 0,
    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,
    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, capacity: usize) !TricacheL3 {
        const entries = try allocator.alloc(CacheEntry, capacity);
        @memset(entries, CacheEntry{});
        log.info("[axicore] TricacheL3 initialized | capacity={d} ({d}KB)", .{
            capacity,
            (capacity * @sizeOf(CacheEntry)) / 1024,
        });
        return .{
            .entries = entries,
            .capacity = capacity,
            .allocator = allocator,
        };
    }
    pub fn deinit(self: *TricacheL3) void {
        self.allocator.free(self.entries);
    }
    pub fn lookup(self: *TricacheL3, key_hash: u64) ?i64 {
        // Linear scan (fully-associative) — in GPU this would be a parallel search
        for (self.entries[0..self.capacity]) |*entry| {
            if (entry.valid and entry.key_hash == key_hash) {
                self.hits += 1;
                entry.age = 0;
                return entry.value;
            }
        }
        self.misses += 1;
        return null;
    }
    pub fn store(self: *TricacheL3, key_hash: u64, value: i64, tag: u32) void {
        // Check if key already exists (update in place)
        for (self.entries[0..self.capacity]) |*entry| {
            if (entry.valid and entry.key_hash == key_hash) {
                entry.value = value;
                entry.age = 0;
                entry.dirty = true;
                return;
            }
        }
        // Find empty slot or LRU victim
        var victim: *CacheEntry = &self.entries[0];
        var max_age: u16 = 0;
        for (self.entries[0..self.capacity]) |*entry| {
            if (!entry.valid) {
                victim = entry;
                break;
            }
            if (entry.age >= max_age) {
                max_age = entry.age;
                victim = entry;
            }
        }
        if (victim.valid) self.evictions += 1;
        victim.* = .{
            .key_hash = key_hash,
            .value = value,
            .tag = tag,
            .valid = true,
        };
        if (self.count < self.capacity) self.count += 1;
        // Periodic age bump
        self.global_age +%= 1;
        if (self.global_age == 0) { // every 65536 stores, age everything
            for (self.entries[0..self.capacity]) |*entry| {
                if (entry.valid) entry.age +|= 1;
            }
        }
    }
    pub fn hitRate(self: *const TricacheL3) f32 {
        const total = self.hits + self.misses;
        if (total == 0) return 0.0;
        return @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.hits)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(total));
    }
};
/// Unified Tricache: hierarchical lookup L1 → L2 → L3
/// Inclusive: data promoted on hit, cascades on store
pub const Tricache = struct {
    l1: TricacheL1 = .{},
    l2: TricacheL2 = .{},
    l3: TricacheL3,
    total_lookups: u64 = 0,
    l1_serves: u64 = 0,
    l2_serves: u64 = 0,
    l3_serves: u64 = 0,
    full_misses: u64 = 0,
    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Tricache {
        return .{
            .l3 = try TricacheL3.init(allocator, TricacheL3.DEFAULT_SIZE),
        };
    }
    pub fn deinit(self: *Tricache) void {
        self.l3.deinit();
    }
    /// Hierarchical lookup: L1 → L2 → L3
    /// On hit at L2/L3, promotes to higher tier (inclusive caching)
    pub fn lookup(self: *Tricache, key_hash: u64) ?i64 {
        self.total_lookups += 1;
        // L1 check (fastest)
        if (self.l1.lookup(key_hash)) |val| {
            self.l1_serves += 1;
            return val;
        }
        // L2 check
        if (self.l2.lookup(key_hash)) |val| {
            self.l2_serves += 1;
            // Promote to L1
            self.l1.store(key_hash, val, 0);
            return val;
        }
        // L3 check (slowest)
        if (self.l3.lookup(key_hash)) |val| {
            self.l3_serves += 1;
            // Promote to L1 and L2
            self.l1.store(key_hash, val, 0);
            self.l2.store(key_hash, val, 0);
            return val;
        }
        self.full_misses += 1;
        return null;
    }
    /// Store at all three tiers (write-through inclusive)
    pub fn store(self: *Tricache, key_hash: u64, value: i64, tag: u32) void {
        self.l1.store(key_hash, value, tag);
        self.l2.store(key_hash, value, tag);
        self.l3.store(key_hash, value, tag);
    }
    /// Store only at L2+L3 (skip L1 for infrequent data)
    pub fn storeCold(self: *Tricache, key_hash: u64, value: i64, tag: u32) void {
        self.l2.store(key_hash, value, tag);
        self.l3.store(key_hash, value, tag);
    }
    pub fn stats(self: *const Tricache) TricacheStats {
        return .{
            .total_lookups = self.total_lookups,
            .l1_hit_rate = self.l1.hitRate(),
            .l2_hit_rate = self.l2.hitRate(),
            .l3_hit_rate = self.l3.hitRate(),
            .overall_hit_rate = if (self.total_lookups == 0) 0.0 else
                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.l1_serves + self.l2_serves + self.l3_serves)) /
                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.total_lookups)),
            .l1_evictions = self.l1.evictions,
            .l2_evictions = self.l2.evictions,
            .l3_evictions = self.l3.evictions,
        };
    }
    pub const TricacheStats = struct {
        total_lookups: u64,
        l1_hit_rate: f32,
        l2_hit_rate: f32,
        l3_hit_rate: f32,
        overall_hit_rate: f32,
        l1_evictions: u64,
        l2_evictions: u64,
        l3_evictions: u64,
    };
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 2. INT1 CONSENSUS — 1-bit Voting, 3-30 Nines of Precision
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// INT1 consensus voting resolves precision arguments:
// - N voters each produce 1-bit answers
// - Majority vote achieves reliability scaling
// - 3 voters → ~3 nines (99.9%)
// - 7 voters → ~7 nines (99.99999%)
// - 15 voters → ~15 nines
// - 31 voters → ~30 nines (for critical compute)
//
// The AI's neural computer uses INT1 consensus for:
// - Verifying memoized results still valid
// - Validating LANG-defined opcode correctness
// - Dream mode sanity checks (is the model hallucinating?)
// - Cross-checking SPZA lookups (angular proximity is fuzzy)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
pub const Int1Consensus = struct {
    /// Precision tier presets
    pub const Tier = enum(u8) {
        quick = 3, // 3 voters → ~3 nines
        standard = 7, // 7 voters → ~7 nines
        high = 15, // 15 voters → ~15 nines
        critical = 31, // 31 voters → ~30 nines
    };
    /// Single voter function: takes inputs, returns 1-bit verdict
    pub const VoterFn = *const fn (a: i64, b: i64, context: u64) bool;
    /// Run consensus vote with N voters
    /// Each voter independently evaluates, majority wins
    /// Returns: (consensus_result, confidence as fraction of agreement)
    pub fn vote(
        voters: []const VoterFn,
        a: i64,
        b: i64,
        context: u64,
    ) ConsensusResult {
        var yes: u32 = 0;
        var no: u32 = 0;
        for (voters) |voter| {
            if (voter(a, b, context)) {
                yes += 1;
            } else {
                no += 1;
            }
        }
        const total = yes + no;
        const majority = total / 2 + 1;
        return .{
            .result = yes >= majority,
            .yes_votes = yes,
            .no_votes = no,
            .confidence = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(@max(yes, no))) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(total)),
            .tier = tierFromCount(@intCast(total)),
        };
    }
    /// Simplified consensus: run the same check N times with different
    /// bit-shifted perspectives (for numeric verification)
    pub fn verifyValue(value: i64, expected: i64, num_voters: u8) ConsensusResult {
        var yes: u32 = 0;
        const n: u32 = @intCast(@min(num_voters, 31));
        for (0..n) |i| {
            // Each voter checks from a different bit perspective
            const shift: u6 = @intCast(i % 64);
            const mask: i64 = @bitCast(@as(u64, 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF) >> shift);
            if ((value & mask) == (expected & mask)) {
                yes += 1;
            }
        }
        return .{
            .result = yes > n / 2,
            .yes_votes = yes,
            .no_votes = n - yes,
            .confidence = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(yes)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(n)),
            .tier = tierFromCount(@intCast(n)),
        };
    }
    /// Verify a memoized result is still valid
    /// Uses consensus to check if cache entry matches recomputation
    pub fn verifyMemo(cached: i64, recomputed: i64, tier: Tier) ConsensusResult {
        return verifyValue(cached, recomputed, @intFromEnum(tier));
    }
    fn tierFromCount(count: u8) Tier {
        if (count >= 31) return .critical;
        if (count >= 15) return .high;
        if (count >= 7) return .standard;
        return .quick;
    }
    pub const ConsensusResult = struct {
        result: bool,
        yes_votes: u32,
        no_votes: u32,
        confidence: f32, // 0.0 - 1.0
        tier: Tier,
        /// Nines of reliability (approximate)
        pub fn nines(self: *const ConsensusResult) u8 {
            // Each doubling of agreeing voters ≈ 1 more nine
            if (self.confidence >= 0.999) return @intCast(@min(self.yes_votes, 30));
            if (self.confidence >= 0.99) return @intCast(@min(self.yes_votes / 2, 15));
            return 1;
        }
    };
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 3. SHIFT-ADD ENGINE — Zero Hardware Multiplies in Hot Paths
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// Every multiply in the neural computer goes through shift-add.
// This includes:
// - ALU MUL instructions (already in alu.zig)
// - SPZA distance calculations
// - Fixed-point scaling operations
// - Canvas coordinate transforms
// - Memoization hash computation
//
// The shift-add engine provides specialized variants:
// - shiftAddMul: general i64 × i64
// - shiftAddMulConst: i64 × compile-time constant (optimized)
// - shiftAddScale: fixed-point scaling by power-of-2 fraction
// - shiftAddDot: vectorized dot product via shift-add
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
pub const ShiftAdd = struct {
    /// General shift-add multiply: a × b without hardware MUL
    /// Decomposes b into powers of 2, shifts a by each set bit, accumulates
    pub fn mul(a: i64, b: i64) i64 {
        const sign_a = a < 0;
        const sign_b = b < 0;
        const abs_a: u64 = if (sign_a) @intCast(-a) else @intCast(a);
        const abs_b: u64 = if (sign_b) @intCast(-b) else @intCast(b);
        var result: u64 = 0;
        var remaining = abs_b;
        var shift: u6 = 0;
        while (remaining != 0) {
            if (remaining & 1 != 0) {
                result +%= abs_a << shift;
            }
            remaining >>= 1;
            if (shift == 63) break;
            shift += 1;
        }
        const signed: i64 = @bitCast(result);
        return if (sign_a != sign_b) -signed else signed;
    }
    /// Compile-time constant multiply optimization
    /// For known constants, decompose at comptime into minimal shift-add chain
    /// e.g. ×1024 = <<10, ×3 = (<<1)+self, ×5 = (<<2)+self, ×7 = (<<3)-self
    pub fn mulConst(a: i64, comptime b: comptime_int) i64 {
        // Special cases the compiler can optimize to single shifts
        if (b == 0) return 0;
        if (b == 1) return a;
        if (b == -1) return -a;
        if (b == 2) return a << 1;
        if (b == 4) return a << 2;
        if (b == 8) return a << 3;
        if (b == 16) return a << 4;
        if (b == 32) return a << 5;
        if (b == 64) return a << 6;
        if (b == 128) return a << 7;
        if (b == 256) return a << 8;
        if (b == 512) return a << 9;
        if (b == 1024) return a << 10;
        // Small odd constants: decompose to shift + add/sub
        if (b == 3) return (a << 1) +% a; // 2a + a
        if (b == 5) return (a << 2) +% a; // 4a + a
        if (b == 6) return (a << 2) +% (a << 1); // 4a + 2a
        if (b == 7) return (a << 3) -% a; // 8a - a
        if (b == 9) return (a << 3) +% a; // 8a + a
        if (b == 10) return (a << 3) +% (a << 1); // 8a + 2a
        if (b == 15) return (a << 4) -% a; // 16a - a
        if (b == 17) return (a << 4) +% a; // 16a + a
        if (b == 255) return (a << 8) -% a; // 256a - a
        if (b == 257) return (a << 8) +% a; // 256a + a
        // Fallback: runtime shift-add
        return mul(a, b);
    }
    /// Fixed-point scaling: a × (num/den) without floating point
    /// Used for SPZA normalization, canvas transforms, etc.
    /// Precision preserved by shifting up first, then dividing
    pub fn scaleFixed(a: i64, num: i64, den: i64) i64 {
        if (den == 0) return 0;
        // Shift up by 32 bits for precision, multiply, shift back
        const wide_a: i128 = @intCast(a);
        const wide_num: i128 = @intCast(num);
        const wide_den: i128 = @intCast(den);
        const result = @divTrunc(wide_a * wide_num, wide_den);
        return @truncate(result);
    }
    /// Vectorized dot product via shift-add per element
    /// Each element multiply is shift-add decomposed
    pub fn dotProduct(a: []const i32, b: []const i32) i64 {
        const len = @min(a.len, b.len);
        var acc: i64 = 0;
        for (0..len) |i| {
            // Shift-add per element pair
            acc +%= mul(@intCast(a[i]), @intCast(b[i]));
        }
        return acc;
    }
    /// Fast hash using only shifts, XORs, and adds (FNV-1a variant)
    /// No multiplies — uses shift-add for the FNV prime multiply
    pub fn hashNoMul(data: []const u8) u64 {
        var h: u64 = 0xcbf29ce484222325; // FNV offset basis
        for (data) |byte| {
            h ^= byte;
            // FNV prime 0x100000001b3 = 2^40 + 2^8 + 0xb3
            // Decompose multiply into shifts+adds:
            const h40 = h << 40;
            const h8 = h << 8;
            const hb3 = (h << 7) +% (h << 5) +% (h << 4) +% (h << 1) +% h; // h×0xB3
            h = h40 +% h8 +% hb3;
        }
        return h;
    }
    /// Generate a cache-friendly hash key from two operands + operation tag
    /// All shift-add, zero multiplies
    pub fn computeKey(a: i64, b: i64, op_tag: u32) u64 {
        var h: u64 = 0xcbf29ce484222325;
        // Mix in operand a
        h ^= @bitCast(a);
        h = (h << 40) +% (h << 8) +% h;
        // Mix in operand b
        h ^= @bitCast(b);
        h = (h << 40) +% (h << 8) +% h;
        // Mix in operation tag
        h ^= @as(u64, op_tag);
        h = (h << 40) +% (h << 8) +% h;
        return h;
    }
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 4. MEP — Minimum Energy Path Routing
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// Borrowed from telecom redundancy/failover concepts applied to compute.
// Every operation has multiple execution paths (pattern of threes):
// Path A: Cached result (zero compute energy)
// Path B: Shift-add compute (low energy)
// Path C: Full precision compute (high energy, fallback)
//
// MEP selects the cheapest path that meets the required precision.
// In dream mode, MEP can be more aggressive (lower precision OK).
// In consensus-critical mode, MEP forces Path C + INT1 verify.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
pub const MEP = struct {
    pub const Path = enum(u2) {
        cached = 0, // Energy: ~0 | Precision: depends on cache freshness
        shift_add = 1, // Energy: ~low | Precision: exact for integers
        full = 2, // Energy: ~high| Precision: maximum
    };
    pub const PrecisionReq = enum(u8) {
        approximate = 0, // Dream mode, exploration — cache OK even if stale
        exact = 1, // Normal compute — shift-add exact for integers
        verified = 2, // Critical — compute + INT1 consensus verify
    };
    /// Route a computation through the minimum energy path
    /// Returns: (result, path_taken)
    pub fn route(
        cache: *Tricache,
        key_hash: u64,
        precision: PrecisionReq,
        compute_fn: *const fn () i64,
    ) struct { value: i64, path: Path } {
        switch (precision) {
            .approximate => {
                // Dream mode: accept any cached value
                if (cache.lookup(key_hash)) |cached| {
                    return .{ .value = cached, .path = .cached };
                }
                // Compute and cache
                const result = compute_fn();
                cache.storeCold(key_hash, result, 0);
                return .{ .value = result, .path = .shift_add };
            },
            .exact => {
                // Normal: check cache, compute on miss
                if (cache.lookup(key_hash)) |cached| {
                    return .{ .value = cached, .path = .cached };
                }
                const result = compute_fn();
                cache.store(key_hash, result, 0);
                return .{ .value = result, .path = .shift_add };
            },
            .verified => {
                // Critical: always compute, verify against cache if present
                const result = compute_fn();
                if (cache.lookup(key_hash)) |cached| {
                    const consensus = Int1Consensus.verifyMemo(cached, result, .standard);
                    if (!consensus.result) {
                        // Cache was stale — update it
                        log.warn("[MEP] cache verification failed | key=0x{X:0>16} cached={d} computed={d}", .{
                            key_hash, cached, result,
                        });
                    }
                }
                cache.store(key_hash, result, 0);
                return .{ .value = result, .path = .full };
            },
        }
    }
    /// Estimate energy cost of a path (relative units)
    pub fn energyCost(path: Path) u32 {
        return switch (path) {
            .cached => 1,
            .shift_add => 10,
            .full => 100,
        };
    }
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 5. SMURFS 4D — Persona State Coordinates
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// SMURFS (Semantic Multi-User Role-based Fusion System) personas
// each have a 4D emotional/cognitive state:
// θ (theta): Emotional valence (-calm ... +excited)
// φ (phi): Cognitive focus (-broad ... +narrow)
// ψ (psi): Confidence level (-uncertain ... +certain)
// τ (tau): Temporal urgency (-patient ... +urgent)
//
// All at 2^60 scale for integer precision.
// The AI's neural computer tracks persona state as it dreams.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
pub const SMURFS_SCALE: i128 = 1 << 60; // 2^60 fixed-point scale
pub const SmurfsState = struct {
    theta: i64 = 0, // emotional valence
    phi: i64 = 0, // cognitive focus
    psi: i64 = 0, // confidence
    tau: i64 = 0, // temporal urgency
    persona_id: u16 = 0,
    active: bool = false,
    dream_depth: u8 = 0, // how deep in dream recursion
    /// Distance between two persona states (for persona switching)
    pub fn distance(self: *const SmurfsState, other: *const SmurfsState) u64 {
        // Manhattan distance (shift-add friendly, no sqrt needed)
        const d_theta: u64 = @intCast(if (self.theta > other.theta) self.theta - other.theta else other.theta - self.theta);
        const d_phi: u64 = @intCast(if (self.phi > other.phi) self.phi - other.phi else other.phi - self.phi);
        const d_psi: u64 = @intCast(if (self.psi > other.psi) self.psi - other.psi else other.psi - self.psi);
        const d_tau: u64 = @intCast(if (self.tau > other.tau) self.tau - other.tau else other.tau - self.tau);
        return d_theta +% d_phi +% d_psi +% d_tau;
    }
    /// Blend two persona states (for smooth transitions)
    /// alpha: 0=100% self, 1024=100% other (fixed-point 10-bit)
    pub fn blend(self: *const SmurfsState, other: *const SmurfsState, alpha: u16) SmurfsState {
        const a: i64 = @intCast(@as(u64, alpha));
        const inv_a: i64 = 1024 - a;
        return .{
            .theta = @divTrunc(ShiftAdd.mul(self.theta, inv_a) +% ShiftAdd.mul(other.theta, a), 1024),
            .phi = @divTrunc(ShiftAdd.mul(self.phi, inv_a) +% ShiftAdd.mul(other.phi, a), 1024),
            .psi = @divTrunc(ShiftAdd.mul(self.psi, inv_a) +% ShiftAdd.mul(other.psi, a), 1024),
            .tau = @divTrunc(ShiftAdd.mul(self.tau, inv_a) +% ShiftAdd.mul(other.tau, a), 1024),
            .persona_id = if (alpha > 512) other.persona_id else self.persona_id,
            .active = true,
            .dream_depth = @max(self.dream_depth, other.dream_depth),
        };
    }
    /// Encode to SPZA coordinate (for spatial indexing of persona states)
    pub fn toSpza(self: *const SmurfsState) core.SpzaCoord {
        return .{
            .dims = .{
                @intCast(self.theta),
                @intCast(self.phi),
                @intCast(self.psi),
                @intCast(self.tau),
                @intCast(self.persona_id),
                @intCast(self.dream_depth),
                0, 0,
            },
        };
    }
};
/// SMURFS persona registry (the AI's inner voices during dream mode)
pub const SmurfsRegistry = struct {
    pub const MAX_PERSONAS = 16;
    personas: [MAX_PERSONAS]SmurfsState = [*]SmurfsState{.{}} ** MAX_PERSONAS,
    active_count: u8 = 0,
    active_persona: u8 = 0, // index of currently speaking persona
    monologue_buffer: [4096]u8 = [_]u8{0} ** 4096, // inner monologue text
    monologue_len: usize = 0,
    /// Activate a persona
    pub fn activate(self: *SmurfsRegistry, id: u8) void {
        if (id >= MAX_PERSONAS) return;
        self.personas[id].active = true;
        self.personas[id].persona_id = id;
        if (self.active_count < MAX_PERSONAS) self.active_count += 1;
    }
    /// Switch to persona with nearest state to target
    pub fn switchNearest(self: *SmurfsRegistry, target: *const SmurfsState) ?u8 {
        var best_dist: u64 = std.math.maxInt(u64);
        var best_idx: ?u8 = null;
        for (self.personas[0..MAX_PERSONAS], 0..) |*p, i| {
            if (!p.active) continue;
            const d = p.distance(target);
            if (d < best_dist) {
                best_dist = d;
                best_idx = @intCast(i);
            }
        }
        if (best_idx) |idx| self.active_persona = idx;
        return best_idx;
    }
    /// Append to inner monologue buffer
    pub fn appendMonologue(self: *SmurfsRegistry, text: []const u8) void {
        const remaining = self.monologue_buffer.len - self.monologue_len;
        const copy_len = @min(text.len, remaining);
        @memcpy(self.monologue_buffer[self.monologue_len .. self.monologue_len + copy_len], text[0..copy_len]);
        self.monologue_len += copy_len;
    }
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 6. HARDWARE DISPATCH — NEON/RKNN2/CUDA/Scalar Auto-Selection
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// axihw layer: the neural computer dispatches to the best available
// hardware backend. On OPi5+ it uses NEON+RKNN2, on RTX it uses CUDA,
// on generic CPU it uses scalar shift-add.
//
// The AI doesn't need to know which hardware it's running on.
// MEP + axihw together ensure optimal execution path.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
pub const HwBackend = enum(u8) {
    scalar = 0, // Pure shift-add, any CPU
    neon = 1, // ARM NEON SIMD (OPi5+, aarch64)
    rknn2 = 2, // Rockchip RKNN2 NPU (RK3588)
    cuda = 3, // NVIDIA CUDA (RTX 5060 Ti, RTX 3060)
    vulkan = 4, // Vulkan compute (cross-platform GPU)
    wasm = 5, // WebAssembly SIMD (browser/edge)
};
pub const HwDispatch = struct {
    primary: HwBackend = .scalar,
    fallback: HwBackend = .scalar,
    detected_backends: u8 = 0, // bitmask of available backends
    /// Auto-detect available hardware
    pub fn detect(self: *HwDispatch) void {
        self.detected_backends = 0;
        self.detected_backends |= (1 << @intFromEnum(HwBackend.scalar)); // always available
        // Compile-time detection via target
        const target = @import("builtin").target;
        if (target.cpu.arch == .aarch64) {
            // ARM64: NEON always available
            self.detected_backends |= (1 << @intFromEnum(HwBackend.neon));
            self.primary = .neon;
            log.info("[axihw] detected NEON (aarch64)", .{});
        }
        if (target.cpu.arch == .x86_64) {
            // x86_64: check for CUDA at runtime
            self.primary = .scalar; // CUDA detection is runtime
            log.info("[axihw] x86_64 detected, CUDA probe at runtime", .{});
        }
        self.fallback = .scalar;
        log.info("[axihw] primary={s} fallback={s} backends=0b{b:0>6}", .{
            @tagName(self.primary),
            @tagName(self.fallback),
            self.detected_backends,
        });
    }
    /// Check if a specific backend is available
    pub fn isAvailable(self: *const HwDispatch, backend: HwBackend) bool {
        return (self.detected_backends & (@as(u8, 1) << @intFromEnum(backend))) != 0;
    }
    /// Select best backend for a given operation type
    pub fn selectBackend(self: *const HwDispatch, op: OpType) HwBackend {
        return switch (op) {
            .scalar_arith => self.primary, // any backend handles this
            .vector_wide => blk: {
                // Prefer GPU for wide vector ops
                if (self.isAvailable(.cuda)) break :blk .cuda;
                if (self.isAvailable(.neon)) break :blk .neon;
                break :blk .scalar;
            },
            .neural_inference => blk: {
                // NPU first, then GPU, then CPU
                if (self.isAvailable(.rknn2)) break :blk .rknn2;
                if (self.isAvailable(.cuda)) break :blk .cuda;
                break :blk .scalar;
            },
            .canvas_render => blk: {
                // GPU strongly preferred for canvas
                if (self.isAvailable(.cuda)) break :blk .cuda;
                if (self.isAvailable(.vulkan)) break :blk .vulkan;
                break :blk .scalar;
            },
        };
    }
    pub const OpType = enum {
        scalar_arith,
        vector_wide,
        neural_inference,
        canvas_render,
    };
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 7. UNIFIED AXICORE CONTEXT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// Single struct holding ALL compute savings primitives.
// Passed to the engine, ALU, and every subsystem.
// The AI's neural computer accesses all of this through one handle.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
pub const AxicoreContext = struct {
    cache: Tricache,
    hw: HwDispatch = .{},
    smurfs: SmurfsRegistry = .{},
    // Global statistics
    total_shift_add_ops: u64 = 0,
    total_cache_saves: u64 = 0, // compute cycles saved by cache hits
    total_consensus_checks: u64 = 0,
    total_mep_routes: u64 = 0,
    energy_saved_estimate: u64 = 0, // relative units of compute energy saved
    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !AxicoreContext {
        var ctx = AxicoreContext{
            .cache = try Tricache.init(allocator),
        };
        ctx.hw.detect();
        log.info("[axicore] context initialized | L1={d} L2={d} L3={d} hw={s}", .{
            TricacheL1.SIZE,
            TricacheL2.SIZE,
            TricacheL3.DEFAULT_SIZE,
            @tagName(ctx.hw.primary),
        });
        return ctx;
    }
    pub fn deinit(self: *AxicoreContext) void {
        self.cache.deinit();
    }
    /// Perform a memoized shift-add multiply through the full pipeline:
    /// 1. Check Tricache hierarchy (L1→L2→L3)
    /// 2. On miss: shift-add compute
    /// 3. Store result in cache
    /// 4. Track energy savings
    pub fn cachedMul(self: *AxicoreContext, a: i64, b: i64) i64 {
        const key = ShiftAdd.computeKey(a, b, 0x4D554C); // "MUL"
        if (self.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.total_cache_saves += 1;
            self.energy_saved_estimate += MEP.energyCost(.shift_add);
            return cached;
        }
        const result = ShiftAdd.mul(a, b);
        self.total_shift_add_ops += 1;
        self.cache.store(key, result, 0x4D554C);
        return result;
    }
    /// Memoized arbitrary operation through Tricache + MEP
    pub fn cachedOp(
        self: *AxicoreContext,
        a: i64,
        b: i64,
        op_tag: u32,
        precision: MEP.PrecisionReq,
        compute_fn: *const fn () i64,
    ) i64 {
        const key = ShiftAdd.computeKey(a, b, op_tag);
        self.total_mep_routes += 1;
        const result = MEP.route(&self.cache, key, precision, compute_fn);
        if (result.path == .cached) {
            self.total_cache_saves += 1;
            self.energy_saved_estimate += MEP.energyCost(.shift_add);
        }
        return result.value;
    }
    /// Get comprehensive savings report
    pub fn savingsReport(self: *const AxicoreContext) SavingsReport {
        const cache_stats = self.cache.stats();
        return .{
            .cache_stats = cache_stats,
            .shift_add_ops = self.total_shift_add_ops,
            .cache_saves = self.total_cache_saves,
            .consensus_checks = self.total_consensus_checks,
            .mep_routes = self.total_mep_routes,
            .energy_saved = self.energy_saved_estimate,
            .hw_backend = self.hw.primary,
        };
    }
    pub const SavingsReport = struct {
        cache_stats: Tricache.TricacheStats,
        shift_add_ops: u64,
        cache_saves: u64,
        consensus_checks: u64,
        mep_routes: u64,
        energy_saved: u64,
        hw_backend: HwBackend,
    };
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// Tests
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
test "tricache: L1 hit" {
    var tc = try Tricache.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer tc.deinit();
    tc.store(0xDEAD, 42, 0);
    const val = tc.lookup(0xDEAD);
    try std.testing.expect(val != null);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), val.?);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), tc.l1_serves);
}
test "tricache: L2 promotion" {
    var tc = try Tricache.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer tc.deinit();
    // Store only in L2 (bypass L1 by filling L1 slot with different key)
    tc.l2.store(0xBEEF, 99, 0);
    tc.l3.store(0xBEEF, 99, 0);
    // L1 has a different key in that slot, so L1 misses
    const val = tc.lookup(0xBEEF);
    try std.testing.expect(val != null);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 99), val.?);
}
test "tricache: full miss" {
    var tc = try Tricache.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer tc.deinit();
    const val = tc.lookup(0x12345);
    try std.testing.expect(val == null);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), tc.full_misses);
}
test "shift-add: multiply" {
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), ShiftAdd.mul(7, 6));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, -42), ShiftAdd.mul(-7, 6));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), ShiftAdd.mul(-7, -6));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 0), ShiftAdd.mul(0, 12345));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 10000), ShiftAdd.mul(100, 100));
}
test "shift-add: mulConst" {
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 30), ShiftAdd.mulConst(10, 3));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 50), ShiftAdd.mulConst(10, 5));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 70), ShiftAdd.mulConst(10, 7));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 10240), ShiftAdd.mulConst(10, 1024));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 2550), ShiftAdd.mulConst(10, 255));
}
test "shift-add: hash no mul" {
    const h1 = ShiftAdd.hashNoMul("hello");
    const h2 = ShiftAdd.hashNoMul("hello");
    const h3 = ShiftAdd.hashNoMul("world");
    try std.testing.expectEqual(h1, h2); // deterministic
    try std.testing.expect(h1 != h3); // different inputs differ
}
test "shift-add: compute key" {
    const k1 = ShiftAdd.computeKey(7, 6, 0x4D554C);
    const k2 = ShiftAdd.computeKey(7, 6, 0x4D554C);
    const k3 = ShiftAdd.computeKey(6, 7, 0x4D554C);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(k1, k2); // same inputs = same key
    try std.testing.expect(k1 != k3); // order matters (not commutative hash)
}
test "int1 consensus: verify exact value" {
    const result = Int1Consensus.verifyValue(42, 42, 7);
    try std.testing.expect(result.result);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 7), result.yes_votes);
}
test "int1 consensus: detect mismatch" {
    const result = Int1Consensus.verifyValue(42, 43, 7);
    // Most voters should detect the difference (lower bits differ)
    try std.testing.expect(result.yes_votes < 7);
}
test "smurfs: persona distance" {
    const a = SmurfsState{ .theta = 100, .phi = 200, .psi = 300, .tau = 400 };
    const b = SmurfsState{ .theta = 150, .phi = 250, .psi = 350, .tau = 450 };
    const d = a.distance(&b);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 200), d); // 50+50+50+50 = 200
}
test "smurfs: persona blend" {
    const a = SmurfsState{ .theta = 0, .phi = 0, .psi = 0, .tau = 0 };
    const b = SmurfsState{ .theta = 1024, .phi = 1024, .psi = 1024, .tau = 1024 };
    const mid = a.blend(&b, 512); // 50/50 blend
    // Should be approximately halfway
    try std.testing.expect(mid.theta > 400 and mid.theta < 600);
}
test "axicore context: cached mul" {
    var ctx = try AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    const r1 = ctx.cachedMul(7, 6); // compute
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r1);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), ctx.total_shift_add_ops);
    const r2 = ctx.cachedMul(7, 6); // cached
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r2);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), ctx.total_cache_saves);
}
test "hw dispatch: detect" {
    var hw = HwDispatch{};
    hw.detect();
    // Scalar always available
    try std.testing.expect(hw.isAvailable(.scalar));
}
test "mep: route cached vs compute" {
    var tc = try Tricache.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer tc.deinit();
    const compute = struct {
        fn f() i64 {
            return 42;
        }
    }.f;
    // First call: compute
    const r1 = MEP.route(&tc, 0xABC, .exact, compute);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r1.value);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(MEP.Path.shift_add, r1.path);
    // Second call: cached
    const r2 = MEP.route(&tc, 0xABC, .exact, compute);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r2.value);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(MEP.Path.cached, r2.path);
}
 
##  
// AxiMinds Neural Computer — ALU (Arithmetic Logic Unit)
// Implements all Tier 0 compute ops via axicore primitives:
// - Native GPU integer ops (ADD, SUB, AND, OR, XOR, shifts)
// - Shift-add decomposition for MUL (avoids expensive multiplier)
// - Memoization for repeated computations
// - SPZA angular distance for spatial ops
//
// Key difference from nCPU: we use ACTUAL arithmetic, not neural inference.
// nCPU: ADD R0,R1,R2 → 8 neural forward passes (~248µs)
// axiNC: ADD R0,R1,R2 → 1 native GPU instruction (~1ns)
const std = @import("std");
const core = @import("../core/types.zig");
const axicore = @import("../core/axicore.zig");
const isa = @import("../isa/opcodes.zig");
const log = std.log.scoped(.axinc_alu);
/// ALU result with flags and savings metadata
pub const AluResult = struct {
    value: i64,
    carry: bool = false,
    overflow: bool = false,
    cache_hit: bool = false, // served from Tricache (L1/L2/L3)?
    mep_path: axicore.MEP.Path = .shift_add, // which energy path was taken?
    energy_cost: u32 = 0, // relative compute energy spent
};
/// Vector ALU result
pub const VecResult = struct {
    values: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32,
    scalar: ?i64 = null, // for reduction ops (VDOT, VRED)
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Scalar ALU — Full axicore compute savings pipeline
//
// Every operation routes through:
// 1. Tricache L1→L2→L3 lookup (cheapest path)
// 2. On miss: ShiftAdd compute (zero hardware MUL)
// 3. INT1 consensus verify (for .verified precision)
// 4. Result stored back into Tricache (all tiers)
// 5. MEP tracks energy savings
//
// The AI's neural computer gets ALL of this, not a subset.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const ScalarAlu = struct {
    ctx: *axicore.AxicoreContext, // full axicore stack
    // Per-ALU statistics
    ops_executed: u64 = 0,
    cache_hits: u64 = 0,
    shift_add_computes: u64 = 0,
    energy_saved: u64 = 0,
    pub fn init(ctx: *axicore.AxicoreContext) ScalarAlu {
        return .{ .ctx = ctx };
    }
    /// ADD: Native addition with overflow detection
    /// ADD is already 1 cycle, no memoization needed (cheaper to compute than lookup)
    pub fn add(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const result = @addWithOverflow(a, b);
        return .{
            .value = result[0],
            .carry = result[1] != 0,
            .overflow = result[1] != 0,
            .mep_path = .shift_add,
            .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add),
        };
    }
    /// SUB: Native subtraction with borrow detection
    pub fn sub(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const result = @subWithOverflow(a, b);
        return .{
            .value = result[0],
            .carry = result[1] != 0,
            .overflow = result[1] != 0,
            .mep_path = .shift_add,
            .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add),
        };
    }
    /// MUL: Full axicore pipeline
    /// Tricache L1→L2→L3 → ShiftAdd → Tricache store
    /// Zero hardware multiplies. All energy tracked.
    pub fn mul(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        // Commutative key: canonical order for better cache hit rate
        const lo = @min(a, b);
        const hi = @max(a, b);
        const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(lo, hi, 0x4D554C);
        // Tricache hierarchical lookup
        if (self.ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.cache_hits += 1;
            self.ctx.total_cache_saves += 1;
            self.energy_saved += axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add);
            return .{
                .value = cached,
                .cache_hit = true,
                .mep_path = .cached,
                .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.cached),
            };
        }
        // Cache miss: shift-add compute (zero hardware MUL)
        const result = axicore.ShiftAdd.mul(a, b);
        self.shift_add_computes += 1;
        self.ctx.total_shift_add_ops += 1;
        // Store in all Tricache tiers
        self.ctx.cache.store(key, result, 0x4D554C);
        return .{
            .value = result,
            .mep_path = .shift_add,
            .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add),
        };
    }
    /// MUL with INT1 consensus verification (for critical paths)
    /// Computes via shift-add, verifies result with N-voter consensus
    pub fn mulVerified(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64, tier: axicore.Int1Consensus.Tier) AluResult {
        const result = self.mul(a, b);
        // Recompute independently for consensus
        const verify = axicore.ShiftAdd.mul(a, b);
        const consensus = axicore.Int1Consensus.verifyMemo(result.value, verify, tier);
        self.ctx.total_consensus_checks += 1;
        if (!consensus.result) {
            log.warn("[ALU] MUL consensus FAILED | a={d} b={d} got={d} verify={d} confidence={d:.3}", .{
                a, b, result.value, verify, consensus.confidence,
            });
            // Return recomputed value on consensus failure
            return .{
                .value = verify,
                .mep_path = .full,
                .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.full),
            };
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// DIV: Iterative shift-subtract division through Tricache
    pub fn div(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) !AluResult {
        if (b == 0) return error.DivisionByZero;
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(a, b, 0x444956); // "DIV"
        if (self.ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.cache_hits += 1;
            self.ctx.total_cache_saves += 1;
            return .{ .value = cached, .cache_hit = true, .mep_path = .cached };
        }
        // Shift-subtract binary long division
        const sign_a = a < 0;
        const sign_b = b < 0;
        const abs_a: u64 = if (sign_a) @intCast(-a) else @intCast(a);
        const abs_b: u64 = if (sign_b) @intCast(-b) else @intCast(b);
        var quotient: u64 = 0;
        var remainder: u64 = 0;
        for (0..64) |i| {
            const bit = 63 - i;
            remainder <<= 1;
            remainder |= (abs_a >> @intCast(bit)) & 1;
            if (remainder >= abs_b) {
                remainder -= abs_b;
                quotient |= @as(u64, 1) << @intCast(bit);
            }
        }
        const result_sign = sign_a != sign_b;
        const signed_result: i64 = if (result_sign)
            -@as(i64, @intCast(quotient))
        else
            @intCast(quotient);
        self.ctx.cache.store(key, signed_result, 0x444956);
        return .{ .value = signed_result, .mep_path = .shift_add };
    }
    /// MOD: Remainder after division, through Tricache
    pub fn mod(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) !AluResult {
        if (b == 0) return error.DivisionByZero;
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(a, b, 0x4D4F44); // "MOD"
        if (self.ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.cache_hits += 1;
            return .{ .value = cached, .cache_hit = true, .mep_path = .cached };
        }
        const result = @rem(a, b);
        self.ctx.cache.store(key, result, 0x4D4F44);
        return .{ .value = result };
    }
    /// Bitwise AND (no cache needed, cheaper to compute)
    pub fn bitAnd(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a & b };
    }
    /// Bitwise OR
    pub fn bitOr(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a | b };
    }
    /// Bitwise XOR
    pub fn bitXor(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a ^ b };
    }
    /// Bitwise NOT
    pub fn bitNot(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = ~a };
    }
    /// Shift left
    pub fn shl(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, shift: u6) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const carry_bit = (a >> @as(u6, @intCast(@as(u7, 63) - @as(u7, shift)))) & 1 != 0;
        return .{ .value = a << shift, .carry = carry_bit };
    }
    /// Shift right (arithmetic)
    pub fn shr(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, shift: u6) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a >> shift };
    }
    /// Compare: subtraction without storing result, only flags
    pub fn cmp(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        return self.sub(a, b);
    }
    /// Increment
    pub fn inc(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        return self.add(a, 1);
    }
    /// Decrement
    pub fn dec(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        return self.sub(a, 1);
    }
    /// Negate
    pub fn neg(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const result = @subWithOverflow(@as(i64, 0), a);
        return .{ .value = result[0], .overflow = result[1] != 0 };
    }
    /// Get ALU performance report
    pub fn report(self: *const ScalarAlu) AluReport {
        const total = self.ops_executed;
        return .{
            .total_ops = total,
            .cache_hits = self.cache_hits,
            .shift_add_computes = self.shift_add_computes,
            .cache_hit_rate = if (total == 0) 0.0 else
                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.cache_hits)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(total)),
            .energy_saved = self.energy_saved,
        };
    }
    pub const AluReport = struct {
        total_ops: u64,
        cache_hits: u64,
        shift_add_computes: u64,
        cache_hit_rate: f32,
        energy_saved: u64,
    };
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Vector ALU — SIMD-width batch operations with axicore savings
// All multiplies route through ShiftAdd. Dot products use shift-add
// per element pair. Maps to NEON/AVX/CUDA warps via HwDispatch.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const VectorAlu = struct {
    /// Element-wise vector addition
    pub fn vadd(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        var result: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = undefined;
        for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
            result[i] = a[i] +% b[i]; // wrapping add for SIMD semantics
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// Element-wise vector subtraction
    pub fn vsub(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        var result: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = undefined;
        for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
            result[i] = a[i] -% b[i];
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// Element-wise vector multiply — ALL through ShiftAdd, zero hardware MUL
    pub fn vmul(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        var result: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = undefined;
        for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
            // Each element multiply is shift-add decomposed
            const product = axicore.ShiftAdd.mul(@intCast(a[i]), @intCast(b[i]));
            result[i] = @truncate(product);
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// Dot product: sum(a[i] * b[i]) → scalar i64
    /// Uses ShiftAdd.dotProduct for zero hardware multiplies
    pub fn vdot(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) i64 {
        return axicore.ShiftAdd.dotProduct(a, b);
    }
    /// Reduction operations
    pub const ReduceOp = enum(u4) {
        sum = 0,
        max = 1,
        min = 2,
        avg = 3,
    };
    pub fn vred(v: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, op: ReduceOp) i64 {
        return switch (op) {
            .sum => blk: {
                var acc: i64 = 0;
                for (v) |elem| acc += @as(i64, elem);
                break :blk acc;
            },
            .max => blk: {
                var m: i32 = std.math.minInt(i32);
                for (v) |elem| m = @max(m, elem);
                break :blk @as(i64, m);
            },
            .min => blk: {
                var m: i32 = std.math.maxInt(i32);
                for (v) |elem| m = @min(m, elem);
                break :blk @as(i64, m);
            },
            .avg => blk: {
                var acc: i64 = 0;
                for (v) |elem| acc += @as(i64, elem);
                break :blk @divTrunc(acc, core.VEC_WIDTH);
            },
        };
    }
    /// Broadcast scalar to all vector lanes
    pub fn vsplat(scalar: i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        return [*]i32{scalar} ** core.VEC_WIDTH;
    }
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// SPZA ALU — Spatial addressing operations
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const SpzaAlu = struct {
    /// Compute angular distance between two SPZA coordinates
    pub fn distance(a: *const core.SpzaCoord, b: *const core.SpzaCoord) u128 {
        return a.angularDistance(b);
    }
    /// Normalize SPZA coordinate to unit sphere at zNorm scale (2^70)
    pub fn normalize(coord: *core.SpzaCoord) void {
        // Compute magnitude via shift-add sqrt approximation
        var sum_sq: u256 = 0;
        inline for (0..8) |i| {
            const v: i256 = @intCast(coord.dims[i]);
            sum_sq += @as(u256, @intCast(if (v < 0) -v else v)) *
                @as(u256, @intCast(if (v < 0) -v else v));
        }
        // Newton-Raphson sqrt via shift-add (axicore style)
        if (sum_sq == 0) return;
        var mag: u256 = 1;
        // Rough initial estimate via leading bit
        var temp = sum_sq;
        var bits: u32 = 0;
        while (temp > 0) : (bits += 1) temp >>= 1;
        mag = @as(u256, 1) << @intCast(bits / 2);
        // 3 Newton iterations (sufficient for our precision)
        for (0..3) |*| {
            if (mag == 0) break;
            mag = (mag + sum_sq / mag) >> 1;
        }
        // Scale each dimension to zNorm (2^70)
        const z_norm: u256 = @as(u256, 1) << 70;
        if (mag == 0) return;
        inline for (0..8) |i| {
            const scaled: i256 = (@as(i256, @intCast(coord.dims[i])) * @as(i256, @intCast(z_norm))) /
                @as(i256, @intCast(mag));
            coord.dims[i] = @truncate(scaled);
        }
        coord.magnitude = @truncate(z_norm);
    }
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Tests
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
test "scalar ALU: add" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = alu.add(40, 2);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(!r.carry);
}
test "scalar ALU: shift-add mul" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = alu.mul(7, 6);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r.value);
}
test "scalar ALU: mul negative" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = alu.mul(-7, 6);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, -42), r.value);
}
test "scalar ALU: mul tricache hit" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    _ = alu.mul(123, 456); // first: compute via shift-add
    const r = alu.mul(123, 456); // second: Tricache L1 hit
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 56088), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(r.cache_hit);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(axicore.MEP.Path.cached, r.mep_path);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), alu.cache_hits);
}
test "scalar ALU: mul commutative cache" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    _ = alu.mul(7, 6); // store with canonical key min(7,6)=6, max=7
    const r = alu.mul(6, 7); // same canonical key: cache hit
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(r.cache_hit);
}
test "scalar ALU: div" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = try alu.div(42, 6);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 7), r.value);
}
test "scalar ALU: div by zero" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    try std.testing.expectError(error.DivisionByZero, alu.div(1, 0));
}
test "scalar ALU: div cached" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    _ = try alu.div(1000, 7);
    const r = try alu.div(1000, 7); // Tricache hit
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 142), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(r.cache_hit);
}
test "scalar ALU: energy tracking" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    _ = alu.mul(10, 20); // shift-add compute
    _ = alu.mul(10, 20); // cache hit: energy saved
    _ = alu.mul(10, 20); // cache hit: more energy saved
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 2), alu.cache_hits);
    try std.testing.expect(alu.energy_saved > 0);
}
test "vector ALU: shift-add dot product" {
    var a: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = [*]i32{0} ** core.VEC_WIDTH;
    var b: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = [*]i32{0} ** core.VEC_WIDTH;
    a[0] = 3;
    a[1] = 4;
    b[0] = 5;
    b[1] = 6;
    const dot = VectorAlu.vdot(&a, &b);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 39), dot); // 3*5 + 4*6 = 39
}
test "vector ALU: reduce sum" {
    var v: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = [_]i32{1} ** core.VEC_WIDTH;
    const sum = VectorAlu.vred(&v, .sum);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, core.VEC_WIDTH), sum);
}
test "vector ALU: splat" {
    const v = VectorAlu.vsplat(42);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 42), v[0]);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 42), v[255]);
}
 
##  
// AxiMinds Neural Computer — Execution Engine
// Fetch → Decode → Execute → Writeback → Hook Check → Loop
//
// This is the heart of axiNC. The engine runs inside the GPU
// alongside the LLM, executing programs the model writes via
// EMIT/LEARN/FUSE/LANG instructions.
//
// Integration: called from llama.cpp FFN tap point each cycle.
const std = @import("std");
const core = @import("../core/types.zig");
const axicore = @import("../core/axicore.zig");
const isa = @import("../isa/opcodes.zig");
const alu_mod = @import("../core/alu.zig");
const log = std.log.scoped(.axinc_exec);
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Execution Engine
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const ExecutionError = error{
    InvalidOpcode,
    MemoryAccessViolation,
    DivisionByZero,
    StackOverflow,
    StackUnderflow,
    ProgramCounterOutOfBounds,
    HookNotAvailable,
    CustomOpcodeNotFound,
    CanvasOutOfBounds,
};
/// Execution trace entry (for debug/introspection)
pub const TraceEntry = struct {
    cycle: u64,
    pc: u64,
    instruction: isa.Instruction,
    result: ?i64 = null,
    memo_hit: bool = false,
    dream_mode: bool = false,
};
/// Execution engine configuration
pub const EngineConfig = struct {
    max_cycles_per_tap: u64 = 1024, // max cycles per FFN tap invocation
    trace_enabled: bool = false,
    trace_buffer_size: usize = 4096,
    memo_enabled: bool = true,
    dream_max_cycles: u64 = 1_000_000,
    self_modify_enabled: bool = true, // allow EMIT/LEARN/FUSE/LANG
};
pub const Engine = struct {
    state: *core.MachineState,
    axicore_ctx: axicore.AxicoreContext,
    scalar_alu: alu_mod.ScalarAlu,
    custom_registry: isa.CustomOpcodeRegistry,
    config: EngineConfig,
    // Trace buffer (ring buffer)
    trace: ?[]TraceEntry = null,
    trace_pos: usize = 0,
    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,
    // Per-tap statistics
    cycles_this_tap: u64 = 0,
    instructions_this_tap: u64 = 0,
    memo_hits_this_tap: u64 = 0,
    pub fn init(
        allocator: std.mem.Allocator,
        state: *core.MachineState,
        config: EngineConfig,
    ) !Engine {
        var trace: ?[]TraceEntry = null;
        if (config.trace_enabled) {
            trace = try allocator.alloc(TraceEntry, config.trace_buffer_size);
        }
        // Initialize full axicore context (Tricache + HwDispatch + SMURFS)
        const ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(allocator);
        log.info("[axiNC] execution engine initialized | max_cycles_per_tap={d} trace={} hw={s}", .{
            config.max_cycles_per_tap,
            config.trace_enabled,
            @tagName(ctx.hw.primary),
        });
        var engine = Engine{
            .state = state,
            .axicore_ctx = ctx,
            .scalar_alu = undefined, // set below
            .custom_registry = .{},
            .config = config,
            .trace = trace,
            .allocator = allocator,
        };
        // ALU must point to Engine's own axicore_ctx (not a stack local)
        engine.scalar_alu = alu_mod.ScalarAlu.init(&engine.axicore_ctx);
        return engine;
    }
    pub fn deinit(self: *Engine) void {
        if (self.trace) |t| self.allocator.free(t);
        self.axicore_ctx.deinit();
    }
    // ── Main Execution Loop ────────────────────────────────────────
    /// Execute cycles until halt, yield, or cycle budget exhausted.
    /// Called from the llama.cpp FFN tap point.
    /// Returns number of cycles executed.
    pub fn executeTap(self: *Engine) !u64 {
        self.cycles_this_tap = 0;
        self.instructions_this_tap = 0;
        self.memo_hits_this_tap = 0;
        self.state.running = true;
        while (self.state.running) {
            // Budget check
            if (self.cycles_this_tap >= self.config.max_cycles_per_tap) {
                break; // yield back to FFN
            }
            // Dream mode cycle countdown
            if (self.state.dream_mode) {
                if (self.state.dream_cycles_remaining == 0) {
                    self.state.wake();
                    break;
                }
                self.state.dream_cycles_remaining -= 1;
            }
            // Fetch
            const pc = self.state.regs.pc;
            const word = self.fetch(pc) catch |err| {
                log.err("[axiNC] fetch error at PC=0x{X:0>8} | {}", .{ pc, err });
                self.state.regs.flags.halted = true;
                self.state.running = false;
                break;
            };
            // Decode
            const instr = isa.Instruction.decode(word);
            // Execute
            self.execute(instr) catch |err| {
                log.err("[axiNC] execute error at PC=0x{X:0>8} | {}", .{ pc, err });
                self.state.regs.flags.halted = true;
                self.state.running = false;
                break;
            };
            // Advance PC (unless a jump already modified it)
            // The execute() function sets a flag if PC was modified
            self.state.regs.cycle_count += 1;
            self.cycles_this_tap += 1;
            self.instructions_this_tap += 1;
            // Check hooks between instructions
            if (self.state.regs.flags.hook_pending) {
                // In dream mode, hooks queue; in run mode, handle immediately
                if (!self.state.dream_mode) {
                    // Hook handling would go here
                    self.state.regs.flags.hook_pending = false;
                }
            }
        }
        self.state.total_cycles += self.cycles_this_tap;
        self.state.total_instructions += self.instructions_this_tap;
        return self.cycles_this_tap;
    }
    // ── Fetch ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn fetch(self: *Engine, pc: u64) !u32 {
        const addr = core.PROGRAM_BASE + pc * 4; // 4 bytes per instruction
        const b0 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr);
        const b1 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr + 1);
        const b2 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr + 2);
        const b3 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr + 3);
        return @as(u32, b0) | (@as(u32, b1) << 8) | (@as(u32, b2) << 16) | (@as(u32, b3) << 24);
    }
    // ── Execute ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn execute(self: *Engine, instr: isa.Instruction) !void {
        const op: isa.Opcode = @enumFromInt(instr.opcode);
        // Trace recording
        if (self.trace) |t| {
            t[self.trace_pos % t.len] = .{
                .cycle = self.state.regs.cycle_count,
                .pc = self.state.regs.pc,
                .instruction = instr,
                .dream_mode = self.state.dream_mode,
            };
            self.trace_pos += 1;
        }
        // Check for custom opcode first
        if (instr.isCustom()) {
            return self.executeCustom(instr);
        }
        switch (op) {
            // ── Scalar Arithmetic ──────────────────────────────────
            .ADD => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.add(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .SUB => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.sub(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .MUL => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.mul(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, r.overflow);
                if (r.cache_hit) self.memo_hits_this_tap += 1;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .DIV => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.div(a, b) catch return error.DivisionByZero;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .SHL => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const shift: u6 = @intCast(instr.imm9 & 0x3F);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.shl(a, shift);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .SHR => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const shift: u6 = @intCast(instr.imm9 & 0x3F);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.shr(a, shift);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .AND => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitAnd(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .OR => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitOr(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .XOR => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitXor(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .NOT => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitNot(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .INC => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.inc(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .DEC => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.dec(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .NEG => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.neg(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .CMP => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.cmp(a, b);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .MOV => {
                const val = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, val);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .MOVI => {
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, @intCast(instr.imm9));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Vector Operations ──────────────────────────────────
            .VADD => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vadd(a, b);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VSUB => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vsub(a, b);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VMUL => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vmul(a, b);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VDOT => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                const dot = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vdot(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, dot);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VRED => {
                const v = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const op: alu_mod.VectorAlu.ReduceOp = @enumFromInt(@as(u4, @intCast(instr.imm9 & 0xF)));
                const result = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vred(v, op);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, result);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VSPLAT => {
                const scalar: i32 = @truncate(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vsplat(scalar);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Memory ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            .LOAD => {
                const addr: u64 = @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                const val = self.state.mem.read64(addr) catch return error.MemoryAccessViolation;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, val);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .STOR => {
                const addr: u64 = @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                const val = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                self.state.mem.write64(addr, val) catch return error.MemoryAccessViolation;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .PUSH => {
                const val = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                self.state.regs.sp -%= 8;
                self.state.mem.write64(self.state.regs.sp, val) catch return error.StackOverflow;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .POP => {
                const val = self.state.mem.read64(self.state.regs.sp) catch return error.StackUnderflow;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, val);
                self.state.regs.sp +%= 8;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Memoization ────────────────────────────────────────
            .MEMO => {
                // Check Tricache hierarchy (L1→L2→L3) first, compute only on miss
                const spza_reg = &self.state.regs.spza[@intCast(instr.rs1 & 0x7)];
                const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(
                    @truncate(spza_reg.dims[0]),
                    @truncate(spza_reg.dims[1]),
                    0x4D454D, // "MEM"
                );
                if (self.axicore_ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
                    self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, cached);
                    self.memo_hits_this_tap += 1;
                } else {
                    // Cache miss: the next instruction computes the value
                    // and the following LEARN stores it
                    self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, 0); // sentinel: miss
                    self.state.regs.flags.zero = true; // flag: memo miss
                }
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Control Flow ───────────────────────────────────────
            .JMP => {
                self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
            },
            .JZ => {
                if (self.state.regs.flags.zero) {
                    self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                } else {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                }
            },
            .JNZ => {
                if (!self.state.regs.flags.zero) {
                    self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                } else {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                }
            },
            .JN => {
                if (self.state.regs.flags.negative) {
                    self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                } else {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                }
            },
            .CALL => {
                // Push return address
                self.state.regs.sp -%= 8;
                const ret_addr: i64 = @intCast(self.state.regs.pc + 1);
                self.state.mem.write64(self.state.regs.sp, ret_addr) catch return error.StackOverflow;
                self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
            },
            .RET => {
                const ret_addr = self.state.mem.read64(self.state.regs.sp) catch return error.StackUnderflow;
                self.state.regs.sp +%= 8;
                self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(ret_addr)));
            },
            .HALT => {
                self.state.regs.flags.halted = true;
                self.state.running = false;
            },
            .YIELD => {
                // Yield back to FFN for one cycle, resume next tap
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                self.state.running = false; // exits executeTap loop
            },
            .NOP => {
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Dream & Canvas ─────────────────────────────────────
            .DREAM => {
                self.state.enterDream(@intCast(instr.imm9));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .WAKE => {
                self.state.wake();
                self.state.running = false; // return to token emission
            },
            .DPIX => {
                const x: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                const y: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                const color_val: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                self.state.canvas.setPixel(x, y, @bitCast(color_val));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Meta / Self-Modification ───────────────────────────
            .EMIT => {
                if (!self.config.self_modify_enabled) {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                    return;
                }
                // Write instruction word from R[rs1] to program address R[rs2]
                const word: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                const addr = core.PROGRAM_BASE + @as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2))) * 4;
                const bytes: [4]u8 = @bitCast(word);
                for (bytes, 0..) |b, i| {
                    self.state.mem.write8(addr + i, b) catch return error.MemoryAccessViolation;
                }
                self.state.regs.flags.self_modify = true;
                self.state.total_fused_ops += 1;
                log.info("[axiNC] EMIT: wrote instruction 0x{X:0>8} at addr 0x{X:0>8}", .{ word, addr });
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .LEARN => {
                if (!self.config.self_modify_enabled) {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                    return;
                }
                // Store value in Tricache at SPZA-derived key
