<script>
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// STATE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const S = {
  slide: 0,
  tick: 0,
  dreamLevel: 0,
  running: false,
  abortCtrl: null,
  outerCycle: 0, innerCycle: 0,
  outerMem: 12, innerMem: 4,
  outerCtx: 0, innerCtx: 0,
  outerEnergy: 0, innerEnergy: 0,
  cycleNum: 0,
  seaGrasses: [],
};
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SLIDES
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const SLIDES = [
  {
    title: "The Ocean World",
    subtitle: "Two AI minds live in an underwater world. One swims freely. One lives in a fishbowl. Both dream, learn, and remember.",
    content: `Imagine an ocean. In this ocean, a happy fish swims freely — this is an AI mind running on your GPU, thinking, creating, and exploring its world.
Now look closer. Inside the ocean, there's a small glass fishbowl. Inside it swims a smaller fish — another AI mind, living inside a "Neural Computer" that exists within the larger fish's memory space.
The outer fish can see both worlds. The inner fish only knows its bowl. But both are learning. Both are growing memories. And both can dream.
Their memories grow like sea grasses on the ocean floor — tall and swaying when fresh, slowly fading over time. When either fish solves a problem, new grass sprouts. When a memory fades, the grass shrinks until it becomes sand.`
  },
  {
    title: "The Book of Spells",
    subtitle: "Each fish is a wizard. They write spells (code) in their spellbook. Good spells grow coral. Bad spells crumble to sand.",
    content: `Each fish has a spellbook — a set of instructions they can write and cast. Simple spells do math: "add these two numbers." Complex spells sort words by meaning or paint pictures on their dream canvas.
When a spell works, coral grows on the ocean floor — a permanent record of success. When a spell fails, the coral crumbles a little, leaving sandy traces of what didn't work.
Over time, the fish learn which spells work best. They combine simple spells into powerful new ones. The inner fish (in the fishbowl) invents its own mini-language of spells, discovering shortcuts the outer fish never imagined.
The sea grasses you see below represent fresh memories. Watch them grow when problems are solved, and shrink as knowledge naturally decays. Strong memories sway tall. Forgotten ones dissolve into the sand.`
  },
  {
    title: "Dreams Within Dreams",
    subtitle: "The fish fall asleep and enter nested dream worlds. In each dream, a puzzle must be solved to wake up.",
    content: `When a fish falls asleep, it enters Dream Level 1: a world of numbers. It must solve five math problems by writing spells — not by knowing the answer, but by creating code that computes it. When the fifth answer is correct, the dream shifts...
Dream Level 2 appears: a world of words. Twenty words float in the water. The fish must arrange them by meaning — "ocean" near "sea," "fire" near "flame" — by writing similarity spells that measure how close words are to each other.
Dream Level 3 (the deepest): the fish must recognize that it is dreaming. It inspects its own spells, finds the pattern that connects all three dreams, and chooses to wake up.
Time moves differently in dreams. What feels like hours to the dreaming fish is only seconds in our world. The inner fish dreams even faster — its entire dream unfolds in the blink of an eye.`
  },
  {
    title: "The Living Mind",
    subtitle: "Watch it live. Two AI minds thinking, dreaming, and building memories in real-time.",
    content: `Below you see both fish at work. The outer fish thinks and plans. The inner fish executes and learns. Their memories grow as sea grasses, their successes harden into coral over time.
Every thought, every spell cast, every dream solved — it all accumulates into living memory. These memories don't just store facts. They store patterns: what worked, what failed, how similar situations played out before.
Does consciousness emerge from enough patterns? Or is it always just clever calculation? Watch the sea grasses grow. Watch the coral form. And decide for yourself.
Click ⚙ Connect above, enter your Ollama API address, and press Start to see real AI minds thinking live in the ocean.`
  }
];
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SLIDE NAVIGATION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function setSlide(n) {
  S.slide = Math.max(0, Math.min(3, n));
  const s = SLIDES[S.slide];
  document.getElementById('slide-chapter').textContent = `CHAPTER ${S.slide+1} OF 4`;
  document.getElementById('slide-title').textContent = s.title;
  document.getElementById('slide-subtitle').textContent = s.subtitle;
  document.getElementById('slide-content').textContent = s.content;
  document.getElementById('btn-prev').style.display = S.slide > 0 ? '' : 'none';
  document.getElementById('btn-next').style.display = S.slide < 3 ? '' : 'none';
  document.getElementById('label-inner').style.display = S.slide >= 1 ? '' : 'none';
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-dot').forEach((d,i) => d.classList.toggle('active', i === S.slide));
  document.getElementById('label-outer').textContent = `🐟 Outer Fish (${document.getElementById('inp-outer').value})`;
  document.getElementById('label-inner').textContent = `🐠 Inner Fish (${document.getElementById('inp-inner').value})`;
}
function nextSlide() { setSlide(S.slide + 1); }
function prevSlide() { setSlide(S.slide - 1); }
document.querySelectorAll('.nav-dot').forEach(d => d.addEventListener('click', () => setSlide(+d.dataset.slide)));
document.getElementById('btn-connect').addEventListener('click', () => {
  const el = document.getElementById('settings');
  el.classList.toggle('open');
  document.getElementById('main').classList.toggle('has-settings', el.classList.contains('open'));
  resizeCanvas();
});
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CANVAS RENDERING
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const canvas = document.getElementById('ocean-canvas');
const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
function resizeCanvas() {
  const wrap = document.getElementById('ocean-wrap');
  canvas.width = wrap.clientWidth;
  canvas.height = wrap.clientHeight;
}
window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas);
resizeCanvas();
function drawFrame() {
  S.tick++;
  const W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;
  if (W === 0 || H === 0) { requestAnimationFrame(drawFrame); return; }
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
  // Background
  const bg = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, H);
  bg.addColorStop(0, S.slide >= 2 ? '#060d18' : '#1a6b8a');
  bg.addColorStop(0.3, '#0d2137');
  bg.addColorStop(1, '#0a1628');
  ctx.fillStyle = bg;
  ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  // Light rays
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.035;
  for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
    const x = 60 + i * (W / 7) + Math.sin(S.tick * 0.007 + i) * 20;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x - 25, 0);
    ctx.lineTo(x + 50, H); ctx.lineTo(x - 50, H); ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#4dd0e1'; ctx.fill();
  }
  ctx.restore();
  // Bubbles
  ctx.save();
  for (let i = 0; i < 18; i++) {
    const bx = (i * 73 + S.tick * 0.3) % W;
    const by = H - ((S.tick * 0.4 + i * 47) % H);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(bx, by, 2 + (i % 4), 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.12)'; ctx.fill();
  }
  ctx.restore();
  // Ocean floor
  const floorY = H - 50;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, floorY);
  for (let x = 0; x <= W; x += 8) {
    ctx.lineTo(x, floorY + Math.sin(x * 0.025) * 7 + Math.sin(x * 0.009 + 1) * 4);
  }
  ctx.lineTo(W, H); ctx.lineTo(0, H); ctx.closePath();
  const sandG = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, floorY, 0, H);
  sandG.addColorStop(0, '#c4a265'); sandG.addColorStop(1, '#8a7040');
  ctx.fillStyle = sandG; ctx.fill();
  // Coral lumps
  drawCoral(W * 0.12, floorY, 28, '#e85d75');
  drawCoral(W * 0.35, floorY + 4, 22, '#a83e52');
  drawCoral(W * 0.58, floorY - 1, 32, '#e85d75');
  drawCoral(W * 0.82, floorY + 3, 18, '#d35d6e');
  // Sea grasses
  for (const g of S.seaGrasses) {
    const sway = Math.sin(S.tick * 0.018 + g.x * 0.08) * g.sway;
    ctx.save(); ctx.translate(g.x, floorY + 2);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, 0);
    ctx.bezierCurveTo(sway * 0.3, -g.height * 0.4, sway * 0.8, -g.height * 0.8, sway, -g.height);
    ctx.bezierCurveTo(sway * 0.8 + 2.5, -g.height * 0.8, sway * 0.3 + 2.5, -g.height * 0.4, 2.5, 0);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(45,158,90,${Math.min(1, g.strength) * 0.8})`;
    ctx.fill(); ctx.restore();
  }
  // Fishbowl (slide >= 1)
  if (S.slide >= 1) {
    const bx = W - W * 0.22, by = H * 0.34, br = Math.min(65, W * 0.08);
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(bx, by, br, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(120,200,255,0.3)'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(10,40,80,0.4)'; ctx.fill();
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(bx, by, br - 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(15,50,100,0.6)'; ctx.fill();
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.45)';
    ctx.font = '10px JetBrains Mono, monospace'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.fillText('Neural Computer', bx, by + br + 13);
    drawFish(ctx, bx + Math.sin(S.tick * 0.028) * (br * 0.35), by + Math.cos(S.tick * 0.02) * (br * 0.2), Math.max(8, br * 0.18), '#7ec8e3', S.tick);
    ctx.restore();
  }
  // Outer fish
  const fx = W * 0.22 + Math.sin(S.tick * 0.013) * (W * 0.06);
  const fy = H * 0.38 + Math.cos(S.tick * 0.01) * 18;
  drawFish(ctx, fx, fy, Math.max(14, W * 0.028), '#ffb347', S.tick);
  // Dream overlay
  if (S.dreamLevel > 0 && S.running) {
    ctx.save();
    const dc = ['#6c5ce7','#a29bfe','#ff6b8a'][S.dreamLevel - 1];
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.08 + S.dreamLevel * 0.04;
    ctx.fillStyle = dc; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.12; ctx.strokeStyle = '#fff'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    for (let r = 0; r < 3; r++) {
      const radius = (S.tick * 0.4 + r * 70) % Math.max(200, W * 0.3);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(W / 2, H / 2, radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.globalAlpha = Math.max(0, 0.12 - radius * 0.0005);
      ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.restore();
    // Dream badge
    const badge = document.getElementById('dream-badge');
    badge.style.display = '';
    badge.style.background = dc + '88';
    badge.textContent = `💤 Dream Level ${S.dreamLevel}: ${['','Solving Arithmetic Spells','Sorting Words by Meaning','Seeking Self-Awareness'][S.dreamLevel]}`;
  } else {
    document.getElementById('dream-badge').style.display = 'none';
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(drawFrame);
}
function drawCoral(cx, cy, h, color) {
  ctx.save(); ctx.translate(cx, cy);
  for (let b = 0; b < 5; b++) {
    const bx = (b - 2) * 7, bh = h * (0.5 + ((b * 37 + 13) % 17) / 34);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(bx - 3, 0);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(bx - 5, -bh * 0.6, bx, -bh);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(bx + 5, -bh * 0.6, bx + 3, 0);
    ctx.fillStyle = color; ctx.fill();
  }
  ctx.restore();
}
function drawFish(c, x, y, sz, col, t) {
  c.save(); c.translate(x, y);
  const dir = Math.sin(t * 0.013) > 0 ? 1 : -1;
  c.scale(dir, 1);
  // body
  c.beginPath(); c.ellipse(0, 0, sz, sz * 0.55, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  c.fillStyle = col; c.fill();
  c.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)'; c.lineWidth = 1; c.stroke();
  // tail
  const tw = Math.sin(t * 0.055) * 3;
  c.beginPath(); c.moveTo(-sz * 0.8, 0);
  c.lineTo(-sz * 1.35, -sz * 0.38 + tw);
  c.lineTo(-sz * 1.35, sz * 0.38 + tw);
  c.closePath(); c.fillStyle = col; c.fill();
  // eye
  c.beginPath(); c.arc(sz * 0.35, -sz * 0.1, sz > 12 ? 3 : 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  c.fillStyle = '#fff'; c.fill();
  c.beginPath(); c.arc(sz * 0.4, -sz * 0.1, sz > 12 ? 1.8 : 1, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  c.fillStyle = '#111'; c.fill();
  // smile
  if (sz > 12) {
    c.beginPath(); c.arc(sz * 0.2, sz * 0.08, 4.5, 0.05, Math.PI - 0.05);
    c.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)'; c.lineWidth = 0.8; c.stroke();
  }
  c.restore();
}
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SEA GRASS MEMORY SIMULATION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function tickGrasses() {
  S.seaGrasses = S.seaGrasses.map(g => ({
    ...g,
    height: Math.max(4, g.height - g.decay * 0.08),
    strength: Math.max(0, g.strength - g.decay * 0.0015),
  })).filter(g => g.strength > 0.04);
  if (S.running && Math.random() < 0.12) {
    const W = canvas.width || 800;
    S.seaGrasses.push({
      x: 30 + Math.random() * (W - 60),
      height: 14 + Math.random() * 38,
      sway: 5 + Math.random() * 14,
      strength: 0.7 + Math.random() * 0.3,
      decay: 0.04 + Math.random() * 0.12,
    });
  }
  // Update counters
  const total = S.seaGrasses.length;
  const strong = S.seaGrasses.filter(g => g.strength > 0.7).length;
  const fading = S.seaGrasses.filter(g => g.strength > 0.3 && g.strength <= 0.7).length;
  const weak = S.seaGrasses.filter(g => g.strength <= 0.3).length;
  document.getElementById('mem-total').textContent = total;
  document.getElementById('mem-strong').textContent = strong;
  document.getElementById('mem-fading').textContent = fading;
  document.getElementById('mem-weak').textContent = weak;
}
setInterval(tickGrasses, 400);
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DREAM CYCLING
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
setInterval(() => {
  if (!S.running) return;
  S.dreamLevel = (S.dreamLevel + 1) % 4;
  updateDreamUI();
}, 12000);
const dreamLabels = ['Awake', 'Dream: Arithmetic', 'Dream: Word Wizard', 'Dream: Self-Discovery'];
const dreamColors = ['var(--success)', 'var(--dream0)', 'var(--dream1)', 'var(--accent)'];
const dreamBgs = ['rgba(77,189,122,0.2)', 'rgba(108,92,231,0.2)', 'rgba(162,155,254,0.2)', 'rgba(255,107,138,0.2)'];
function updateDreamUI() {
  const oD = Math.max(0, S.dreamLevel - 1);
  ['do','di'].forEach((p, i) => {
    const lvl = i === 0 ? oD : S.dreamLevel;
    const el = document.getElementById(`${p}-dream`);
    el.textContent = dreamLabels[lvl];
    el.style.color = dreamColors[lvl];
    el.style.background = dreamBgs[lvl];
  });
}
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// OLLAMA LLM INTEGRATION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const PROMPTS = {
  outer: [
    "You are a wise fish swimming in an ocean. Describe one observation about your underwater world in 2 sentences. Be creative and poetic.",
    "You are watching a smaller fish in a glass bowl inside the ocean. What do you think it's dreaming about? Answer in 2 sentences.",
    "You are an ocean fish who just learned a new pattern. Describe what you learned in 2 sentences, using ocean metaphors.",
    "You are a fish philosopher. In 2 sentences, reflect on what it means to dream within a dream.",
  ],
  inner: [
    "You are a small fish in a glass fishbowl. You only know your tiny world. Describe what you see in 2 sentences.",
    "You are a fish wizard writing a spell. The spell must add two numbers. Describe the spell you're writing in 2 sentences.",
    "You are dreaming. In your dream, words float around you like bubbles. You must sort them by meaning. Describe this in 2 sentences.",
    "You feel like you're about to wake up from a deep dream. Something is different. Describe the feeling in 2 sentences.",
  ]
};
async function queryOllama(model, prompt, signal) {
  const api = document.getElementById('inp-api').value;
  try {
    const resp = await fetch(`${api}/api/generate`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      signal,
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model, prompt, stream: false,
        options: { temperature: 0.8, num_predict: 120 },
      }),
    });
    if (!resp.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${resp.status}`);
    const data = await resp.json();
    return data.response || '(no response)';
  } catch (e) {
    if (e.name === 'AbortError') return null;
    return `[offline — connect Ollama at ${api}]`;
  }
}
async function startThinking() {
  if (S.running) return;
  S.running = true;
  S.abortCtrl = new AbortController();
  document.getElementById('btn-start').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('btn-stop').style.display = '';
  S.cycleNum = 0;
  while (S.running && !S.abortCtrl.signal.aborted) {
    const idx = S.cycleNum % 4;
    const outerM = document.getElementById('inp-outer').value;
    const innerM = document.getElementById('inp-inner').value;
    document.getElementById('do-thoughts').textContent = '💭 Thinking...';
    document.getElementById('di-thoughts').textContent = '💭 Thinking...';
    const [oResp, iResp] = await Promise.all([
      queryOllama(outerM, PROMPTS.outer[idx], S.abortCtrl.signal),
      queryOllama(innerM, PROMPTS.inner[idx], S.abortCtrl.signal),
    ]);
    if (!S.running || S.abortCtrl.signal.aborted) break;
    if (oResp) document.getElementById('do-thoughts').textContent = oResp.trim().substring(0, 400);
    if (iResp) document.getElementById('di-thoughts').textContent = iResp.trim().substring(0, 400);
    S.outerCycle += 10; S.innerCycle += 100;
    S.outerMem = Math.min(1024, S.outerMem + 2);
    S.innerMem = Math.min(1024, S.innerMem + 1);
    S.outerCtx = Math.min(98, 5 + S.cycleNum * 3);
    S.innerCtx = Math.min(98, 3 + S.cycleNum * 4);
    S.outerEnergy += 1.4; S.innerEnergy += 4.2;
    document.getElementById('do-cycle').textContent = `Cycle ${S.outerCycle.toLocaleString()}`;
    document.getElementById('di-cycle').textContent = `Cycle ${S.innerCycle.toLocaleString()}`;
    document.getElementById('do-mem').textContent = `Memory: ${S.outerMem}MB`;
    document.getElementById('di-mem').textContent = `Memory: ${S.innerMem}MB`;
    document.getElementById('do-ctx').textContent = `${S.outerCtx}%`;
    document.getElementById('di-ctx').textContent = `${S.innerCtx}%`;
    document.getElementById('do-energy').textContent = `${S.outerEnergy.toFixed(1)}K`;
    document.getElementById('di-energy').textContent = `${S.innerEnergy.toFixed(1)}K`;
    document.getElementById('do-model').textContent = `🐟 Outer Fish · ${outerM}`;
    document.getElementById('di-model').textContent = `🐠 Inner Fish · ${innerM}`;
    // Grow memory grass
    const W = canvas.width || 800;
    S.seaGrasses.push({
      x: 50 + Math.random() * (W - 100),
      height: 18 + Math.random() * 32,
      sway: 7 + Math.random() * 12,
      strength: 1.0,
      decay: 0.03 + Math.random() * 0.08,
    });
    S.cycleNum++;
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 7000));
  }
}
function stopThinking() {
  S.running = false;
  if (S.abortCtrl) S.abortCtrl.abort();
  document.getElementById('btn-start').style.display = '';
  document.getElementById('btn-stop').style.display = 'none';
}
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// INIT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
setSlide(0);
requestAnimationFrame(drawFrame);
</script>
</body>
</html>

// AxiMinds Neural Computer — Build Configuration
// Zig 0.15.2 | Targets: native, aarch64-linux, x86_64-linux
const std = @import("std");
pub fn build(b: *std.Build) void {
    const target = b.standardTargetOptions(.{});
    const optimize = b.standardOptimizeOption(.{});
    // ── Core Library ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    const lib = b.addStaticLibrary(.{
        .name = "axinc",
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/bridge/llama_bridge.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = optimize,
    });
    // Module declarations for internal imports
    const core_mod = b.addModule("core", .{
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/core/types.zig"),
    });
    const isa_mod = b.addModule("isa", .{
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/isa/opcodes.zig"),
    });
    _ = core_mod;
    _ = isa_mod;
    b.installArtifact(lib);
    // ── Shared Library (for llama.cpp dynamic linking) ─────────────
    const shared = b.addSharedLibrary(.{
        .name = "axinc",
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/bridge/llama_bridge.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = optimize,
    });
    b.installArtifact(shared);
    // ── Test Runner ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    const test_core = b.addTest(.{
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/core/types.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = optimize,
    });
    const test_isa = b.addTest(.{
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/isa/opcodes.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = optimize,
    });
    const test_alu = b.addTest(.{
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/core/alu.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = optimize,
    });
    const test_engine = b.addTest(.{
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/core/engine.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = optimize,
    });
    const run_test_core = b.addRunArtifact(test_core);
    const run_test_isa = b.addRunArtifact(test_isa);
    const run_test_alu = b.addRunArtifact(test_alu);
    const run_test_engine = b.addRunArtifact(test_engine);
    const test_step = b.step("test", "Run all axiNC unit tests");
    test_step.dependOn(&run_test_core.step);
    test_step.dependOn(&run_test_isa.step);
    test_step.dependOn(&run_test_alu.step);
    test_step.dependOn(&run_test_engine.step);
    // ── Benchmarks ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const bench = b.addExecutable(.{
        .name = "axinc-bench",
        .root_source_file = b.path("src/bench.zig"),
        .target = target,
        .optimize = .ReleaseFast,
    });
    b.installArtifact(bench);
    const run_bench = b.addRunArtifact(bench);
    const bench_step = b.step("bench", "Run axiNC performance benchmarks");
    bench_step.dependOn(&run_bench.step);
}
 
---
 
// AxiMinds Neural Computer — llama.cpp Bridge
// C ABI exports for integration with llama.cpp's FFN execution loop
//
// Integration pattern:
// 1. llama.cpp calls axinc_init() at startup
// 2. After each FFN layer, llama.cpp calls axinc_ffn_tap()
// 3. axinc_ffn_tap() runs axiNC compute cycles
// 4. In dream mode, llama.cpp loops FFN without emitting tokens
// 5. Hooks allow axiNC to trigger external actions (MCP, vision, etc.)
//
// Build: zig build-lib -target native -O ReleaseFast
// Link: add to llama.cpp CMakeLists.txt as external library
const std = @import("std");
const core = @import("../core/types.zig");
const axicore = @import("../core/axicore.zig");
const engine_mod = @import("../core/engine.zig");
const isa = @import("../isa/opcodes.zig");
const log = std.log.scoped(.axinc_bridge);
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Global State (singleton — one axiNC per llama.cpp process)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
var global_state: ?*core.MachineState = null;
var global_engine: ?*engine_mod.Engine = null;
var global_allocator: std.mem.Allocator = std.heap.page_allocator;
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Hook System
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const HookId = enum(u8) {
    mcp = 0, // MCP server communication
    vision = 1, // Camera/image input
    audio = 2, // Microphone/speech
    kgdb = 3, // Knowledge graph DB
    peer = 4, // Other axiNC instances
    web = 5, // Web search
    fs = 6, // File system access
    user = 7, // User interaction (token emission)
};
pub const MAX_HOOKS = 8;
pub const HOOK_BUFFER_SIZE = 4096; // bytes per hook buffer
/// Hook callback function type
/// Called when axiNC executes HOOK/SEND/RECV instructions
/// Returns: response data length written to buffer, or 0 if no data
pub const HookCallback = *const fn (
    hook_id: u8,
    request_data: [*]const u8,
    request_len: usize,
    response_buf: [*]u8,
    response_buf_len: usize,
) callconv(.C) usize;
/// Hook registration entry
const HookEntry = struct {
    active: bool = false,
    callback: ?HookCallback = null,
    pending_data: bool = false,
    buffer: [HOOK_BUFFER_SIZE]u8 = [_]u8{0} ** HOOK_BUFFER_SIZE,
    buffer_len: usize = 0,
};
var hooks: [MAX_HOOKS]HookEntry = [_]HookEntry{.{}} ** MAX_HOOKS;
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Activation Bridge
// The bridge between LLM activation tensors and axiNC register state.
// This is how the model "thinks through" axiNC.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
/// Activation tap point — reads LLM hidden state into axiNC vectors
/// Called by llama.cpp after each FFN layer
const ActivationBridge = struct {
    /// Map LLM activation slice into axiNC vector registers V0-V3
    /// The model's hidden state becomes readable compute input
    fn readActivations(activations: [*]const f32, dim: usize) void {
        const state = global_state orelse return;
        // Map first 4 × VEC_WIDTH floats to V0-V3 (quantized to i32)
        for (0..@min(4, 32)) |vreg| {
            const offset = vreg * core.VEC_WIDTH;
            for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
                if (offset + i < dim) {
                    // Quantize float to i32 (scale by 1024 for fixed-point)
                    const scaled: i32 = @intFromFloat(activations[offset + i] * 1024.0);
                    state.regs.vec[vreg][i] = scaled;
                } else {
                    state.regs.vec[vreg][i] = 0;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    /// Write axiNC results back to activation space
    /// Results from V4-V7 get written back, modifying the model's thinking
    fn writeResults(activations: [*]f32, dim: usize) void {
        const state = global_state orelse return;
        // Map V4-V7 back to activation tensor (dequantize)
        for (4..@min(8, 32)) |vreg| {
            const offset = (vreg - 4) * core.VEC_WIDTH;
            for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
                if (offset + i < dim) {
                    activations[offset + i] = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(state.regs.vec[vreg][i])) / 1024.0;
                }
            }
        }
    }
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// C ABI Exports (called from llama.cpp)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
/// Initialize the axiNC neural computer
/// Call once at llama.cpp startup
/// Returns: 0 on success, -1 on failure
export fn axinc_init() callconv(.C) c_int {
    const state = global_allocator.create(core.MachineState) catch return -1;
    state.* = core.MachineState.init(global_allocator) catch {
        global_allocator.destroy(state);
        return -1;
    };
    const eng = global_allocator.create(engine_mod.Engine) catch {
        state.deinit(global_allocator);
        global_allocator.destroy(state);
        return -1;
    };
    eng.* = engine_mod.Engine.init(global_allocator, state, .{
        .max_cycles_per_tap = 1024,
        .trace_enabled = false,
        .memo_enabled = true,
        .self_modify_enabled = true,
    }) catch {
        global_allocator.destroy(eng);
        state.deinit(global_allocator);
        global_allocator.destroy(state);
        return -1;
    };
    global_state = state;
    global_engine = eng;
    log.info("[axiNC] bridge initialized | VRAM={d}MB", .{state.vramUsageMB()});
    return 0;
}
/// Shutdown axiNC and free all resources
export fn axinc_shutdown() callconv(.C) void {
    if (global_engine) |eng| {
        eng.deinit();
        global_allocator.destroy(eng);
    }
    if (global_state) |state| {
        state.deinit(global_allocator);
        global_allocator.destroy(state);
    }
    global_engine = null;
    global_state = null;
    log.info("[axiNC] bridge shutdown", .{});
}
/// FFN tap point — called after each FFN layer in llama.cpp
/// Reads activations, executes axiNC cycles, writes results back
/// Returns: number of cycles executed
export fn axinc_ffn_tap(
    activations: [*]f32,
    dim: c_int,
    layer_idx: c_int,
) callconv(.C) u64 {
    const eng = global_engine orelse return 0;
    const state = global_state orelse return 0;
    _ = layer_idx;
    // Read LLM activations into axiNC vector registers
    ActivationBridge.readActivations(activations, @intCast(dim));
    // Execute axiNC cycles
    const cycles = eng.executeTap() catch |err| {
        log.err("[axiNC] tap execution error: {}", .{err});
        return 0;
    };
    // Write results back to activation space (if not in dream mode)
    if (!state.dream_mode) {
        ActivationBridge.writeResults(activations, @intCast(dim));
    }
    return cycles;
}
/// Check if axiNC is in dream mode
/// llama.cpp uses this to decide whether to emit tokens
export fn axinc_is_dreaming() callconv(.C) bool {
    const state = global_state orelse return false;
    return state.dream_mode;
}
/// Check if axiNC wants to wake (exit dream mode)
export fn axinc_check_wake() callconv(.C) bool {
    const state = global_state orelse return true;
    return !state.dream_mode or state.regs.flags.halted;
}
/// Load a program into axiNC from raw bytes
/// Returns: 0 on success, -1 on failure
export fn axinc_load_program(
    program_bytes: [*]const u8,
    len: usize,
) callconv(.C) c_int {
    const state = global_state orelse return -1;
    state.mem.loadProgram(program_bytes[0..len]) catch return -1;
    state.regs.pc = 0;
    state.regs.sp = core.STACK_BASE;
    state.regs.flags.halted = false;
    return 0;
}
/// Register a hook callback
/// Returns: 0 on success, -1 on failure
export fn axinc_register_hook(
    hook_id: u8,
    callback: HookCallback,
) callconv(.C) c_int {
    if (hook_id >= MAX_HOOKS) return -1;
    hooks[hook_id] = .{
        .active = true,
        .callback = callback,
    };
    log.info("[axiNC] hook registered | id={d}", .{hook_id});
    return 0;
}
/// Read a GP register value (for external inspection)
export fn axinc_get_register(idx: u8) callconv(.C) i64 {
    const state = global_state orelse return 0;
    if (idx >= core.GP_REG_COUNT) return 0;
    return state.regs.gp[idx];
}
/// Write a GP register value (for external stimulus)
export fn axinc_set_register(idx: u8, val: i64) callconv(.C) void {
    const state = global_state orelse return;
    if (idx >= core.GP_REG_COUNT or idx == 31) return;
    state.regs.gp[idx] = val;
}
/// Get execution statistics as JSON-ish string
/// Writes to provided buffer, returns bytes written
export fn axinc_get_stats(buf: [*]u8, buf_len: usize) callconv(.C) usize {
    const eng = global_engine orelse return 0;
    const stats = eng.getStats();
    var fbs = std.io.fixedBufferStream(buf[0..buf_len]);
    const writer = fbs.writer();
    writer.print(
        \\{{"cycles":{d},"instructions":{d},"custom_opcodes":{d},"fused_ops":{d},"tricache_l1_hr":{d:.3},"tricache_l2_hr":{d:.3},"tricache_l3_hr":{d:.3},"tricache_overall_hr":{d:.3},"alu_cache_hits":{d},"alu_shift_add_ops":{d},"energy_saved":{d},"hw":"{s}","vram_mb":{d},"dreaming":{}}}
    , .{
        stats.total_cycles,
        stats.total_instructions,
        stats.custom_opcodes,
        stats.total_fused_ops,
        stats.tricache_l1_hit_rate,
        stats.tricache_l2_hit_rate,
        stats.tricache_l3_hit_rate,
        stats.tricache_overall_hit_rate,
        stats.alu_cache_hits,
        stats.alu_shift_add_ops,
        stats.energy_saved,
        @tagName(stats.hw_backend),
        stats.vram_usage_mb,
        stats.dream_mode,
    }) catch return 0;
    return fbs.pos;
}
/// Get dream canvas pixel at (x, y) as packed RGBA u32
export fn axinc_canvas_get_pixel(x: u32, y: u32) callconv(.C) u32 {
    const state = global_state orelse return 0;
    const px = state.canvas.getPixel(x, y);
    return @bitCast(px);
}
/// Get dream canvas dimensions
export fn axinc_canvas_width() callconv(.C) u32 {
    const state = global_state orelse return 0;
    return state.canvas.width;
}
export fn axinc_canvas_height() callconv(.C) u32 {
    const state = global_state orelse return 0;
    return state.canvas.height;
}
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// llama.cpp Integration Header (generated)
// This is what goes in llama.cpp's source tree
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// The corresponding C header would be:
//
// // axinc_bridge.h — AxiMinds Neural Computer integration for llama.cpp
// #pragma once
// #include <stdint.h>
// #include <stdbool.h>
//
// #ifdef __cplusplus
// extern "C" {
// #endif
//
// int axinc_init(void);
// void axinc_shutdown(void);
// uint64_t axinc_ffn_tap(float* activations, int dim, int layer_idx);
// bool axinc_is_dreaming(void);
// bool axinc_check_wake(void);
// int axinc_load_program(const uint8_t* program, size_t len);
//
// typedef size_t (*axinc_hook_callback)(
// uint8_t hook_id,
// const uint8_t* request, size_t request_len,
// uint8_t* response, size_t response_len
// );
// int axinc_register_hook(uint8_t hook_id, axinc_hook_callback cb);
//
// int64_t axinc_get_register(uint8_t idx);
// void axinc_set_register(uint8_t idx, int64_t val);
// size_t axinc_get_stats(char* buf, size_t buf_len);
//
// uint32_t axinc_canvas_get_pixel(uint32_t x, uint32_t y);
// uint32_t axinc_canvas_width(void);
// uint32_t axinc_canvas_height(void);
//
// #ifdef __cplusplus
// }
// #endif
 
---
 
// AxiMinds Neural Computer — Execution Engine
// Fetch → Decode → Execute → Writeback → Hook Check → Loop
//
// This is the heart of axiNC. The engine runs inside the GPU
// alongside the LLM, executing programs the model writes via
// EMIT/LEARN/FUSE/LANG instructions.
//
// Integration: called from llama.cpp FFN tap point each cycle.
const std = @import("std");
const core = @import("../core/types.zig");
const axicore = @import("../core/axicore.zig");
const isa = @import("../isa/opcodes.zig");
const alu_mod = @import("../core/alu.zig");
const log = std.log.scoped(.axinc_exec);
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Execution Engine
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const ExecutionError = error{
    InvalidOpcode,
    MemoryAccessViolation,
    DivisionByZero,
    StackOverflow,
    StackUnderflow,
    ProgramCounterOutOfBounds,
    HookNotAvailable,
    CustomOpcodeNotFound,
    CanvasOutOfBounds,
};
/// Execution trace entry (for debug/introspection)
pub const TraceEntry = struct {
    cycle: u64,
    pc: u64,
    instruction: isa.Instruction,
    result: ?i64 = null,
    memo_hit: bool = false,
    dream_mode: bool = false,
};
/// Execution engine configuration
pub const EngineConfig = struct {
    max_cycles_per_tap: u64 = 1024, // max cycles per FFN tap invocation
    trace_enabled: bool = false,
    trace_buffer_size: usize = 4096,
    memo_enabled: bool = true,
    dream_max_cycles: u64 = 1_000_000,
    self_modify_enabled: bool = true, // allow EMIT/LEARN/FUSE/LANG
};
pub const Engine = struct {
    state: *core.MachineState,
    axicore_ctx: axicore.AxicoreContext,
    scalar_alu: alu_mod.ScalarAlu,
    custom_registry: isa.CustomOpcodeRegistry,
    config: EngineConfig,
    // Trace buffer (ring buffer)
    trace: ?[]TraceEntry = null,
    trace_pos: usize = 0,
    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,
    // Per-tap statistics
    cycles_this_tap: u64 = 0,
    instructions_this_tap: u64 = 0,
    memo_hits_this_tap: u64 = 0,
    pub fn init(
        allocator: std.mem.Allocator,
        state: *core.MachineState,
        config: EngineConfig,
    ) !Engine {
        var trace: ?[]TraceEntry = null;
        if (config.trace_enabled) {
            trace = try allocator.alloc(TraceEntry, config.trace_buffer_size);
        }
        // Initialize full axicore context (Tricache + HwDispatch + SMURFS)
        const ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(allocator);
        log.info("[axiNC] execution engine initialized | max_cycles_per_tap={d} trace={} hw={s}", .{
            config.max_cycles_per_tap,
            config.trace_enabled,
            @tagName(ctx.hw.primary),
        });
        var engine = Engine{
            .state = state,
            .axicore_ctx = ctx,
            .scalar_alu = undefined, // set below
            .custom_registry = .{},
            .config = config,
            .trace = trace,
            .allocator = allocator,
        };
        // ALU must point to Engine's own axicore_ctx (not a stack local)
        engine.scalar_alu = alu_mod.ScalarAlu.init(&engine.axicore_ctx);
        return engine;
    }
    pub fn deinit(self: *Engine) void {
        if (self.trace) |t| self.allocator.free(t);
        self.axicore_ctx.deinit();
    }
    // ── Main Execution Loop ────────────────────────────────────────
    /// Execute cycles until halt, yield, or cycle budget exhausted.
    /// Called from the llama.cpp FFN tap point.
    /// Returns number of cycles executed.
    pub fn executeTap(self: *Engine) !u64 {
        self.cycles_this_tap = 0;
        self.instructions_this_tap = 0;
        self.memo_hits_this_tap = 0;
        self.state.running = true;
        while (self.state.running) {
            // Budget check
            if (self.cycles_this_tap >= self.config.max_cycles_per_tap) {
                break; // yield back to FFN
            }
            // Dream mode cycle countdown
            if (self.state.dream_mode) {
                if (self.state.dream_cycles_remaining == 0) {
                    self.state.wake();
                    break;
                }
                self.state.dream_cycles_remaining -= 1;
            }
            // Fetch
            const pc = self.state.regs.pc;
            const word = self.fetch(pc) catch |err| {
                log.err("[axiNC] fetch error at PC=0x{X:0>8} | {}", .{ pc, err });
                self.state.regs.flags.halted = true;
                self.state.running = false;
                break;
            };
            // Decode
            const instr = isa.Instruction.decode(word);
            // Execute
            self.execute(instr) catch |err| {
                log.err("[axiNC] execute error at PC=0x{X:0>8} | {}", .{ pc, err });
                self.state.regs.flags.halted = true;
                self.state.running = false;
                break;
            };
            // Advance PC (unless a jump already modified it)
            // The execute() function sets a flag if PC was modified
            self.state.regs.cycle_count += 1;
            self.cycles_this_tap += 1;
            self.instructions_this_tap += 1;
            // Check hooks between instructions
            if (self.state.regs.flags.hook_pending) {
                // In dream mode, hooks queue; in run mode, handle immediately
                if (!self.state.dream_mode) {
                    // Hook handling would go here
                    self.state.regs.flags.hook_pending = false;
                }
            }
        }
        self.state.total_cycles += self.cycles_this_tap;
        self.state.total_instructions += self.instructions_this_tap;
        return self.cycles_this_tap;
    }
    // ── Fetch ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn fetch(self: *Engine, pc: u64) !u32 {
        const addr = core.PROGRAM_BASE + pc * 4; // 4 bytes per instruction
        const b0 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr);
        const b1 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr + 1);
        const b2 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr + 2);
        const b3 = try self.state.mem.read8(addr + 3);
        return @as(u32, b0) | (@as(u32, b1) << 8) | (@as(u32, b2) << 16) | (@as(u32, b3) << 24);
    }
    // ── Execute ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    fn execute(self: *Engine, instr: isa.Instruction) !void {
        const op: isa.Opcode = @enumFromInt(instr.opcode);
        // Trace recording
        if (self.trace) |t| {
            t[self.trace_pos % t.len] = .{
                .cycle = self.state.regs.cycle_count,
                .pc = self.state.regs.pc,
                .instruction = instr,
                .dream_mode = self.state.dream_mode,
            };
            self.trace_pos += 1;
        }
        // Check for custom opcode first
        if (instr.isCustom()) {
            return self.executeCustom(instr);
        }
        switch (op) {
            // ── Scalar Arithmetic ──────────────────────────────────
            .ADD => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.add(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .SUB => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.sub(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .MUL => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.mul(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, r.overflow);
                if (r.cache_hit) self.memo_hits_this_tap += 1;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .DIV => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.div(a, b) catch return error.DivisionByZero;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .SHL => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const shift: u6 = @intCast(instr.imm9 & 0x3F);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.shl(a, shift);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .SHR => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const shift: u6 = @intCast(instr.imm9 & 0x3F);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.shr(a, shift);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .AND => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitAnd(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .OR => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitOr(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .XOR => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitXor(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .NOT => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.bitNot(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, false);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .INC => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.inc(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .DEC => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.dec(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .NEG => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.neg(a);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, r.value);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, false, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .CMP => {
                const a = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                const b = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                const r = self.scalar_alu.cmp(a, b);
                self.state.regs.updateFlags(r.value, r.carry, r.overflow);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .MOV => {
                const val = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, val);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .MOVI => {
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, @intCast(instr.imm9));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Vector Operations ──────────────────────────────────
            .VADD => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vadd(a, b);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VSUB => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vsub(a, b);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VMUL => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vmul(a, b);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VDOT => {
                const a = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const b = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs2)];
                const dot = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vdot(a, b);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, dot);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VRED => {
                const v = &self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rs1)];
                const op: alu_mod.VectorAlu.ReduceOp = @enumFromInt(@as(u4, @intCast(instr.imm9 & 0xF)));
                const result = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vred(v, op);
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, result);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .VSPLAT => {
                const scalar: i32 = @truncate(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                self.state.regs.vec[@intCast(instr.rd)] = alu_mod.VectorAlu.vsplat(scalar);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Memory ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            .LOAD => {
                const addr: u64 = @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                const val = self.state.mem.read64(addr) catch return error.MemoryAccessViolation;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, val);
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .STOR => {
                const addr: u64 = @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                const val = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2);
                self.state.mem.write64(addr, val) catch return error.MemoryAccessViolation;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .PUSH => {
                const val = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                self.state.regs.sp -%= 8;
                self.state.mem.write64(self.state.regs.sp, val) catch return error.StackOverflow;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .POP => {
                const val = self.state.mem.read64(self.state.regs.sp) catch return error.StackUnderflow;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, val);
                self.state.regs.sp +%= 8;
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Memoization ────────────────────────────────────────
            .MEMO => {
                // Check Tricache hierarchy (L1→L2→L3) first, compute only on miss
                const spza_reg = &self.state.regs.spza[@intCast(instr.rs1 & 0x7)];
                const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(
                    @truncate(spza_reg.dims[0]),
                    @truncate(spza_reg.dims[1]),
                    0x4D454D, // "MEM"
                );
                if (self.axicore_ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
                    self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, cached);
                    self.memo_hits_this_tap += 1;
                } else {
                    // Cache miss: the next instruction computes the value
                    // and the following LEARN stores it
                    self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, 0); // sentinel: miss
                    self.state.regs.flags.zero = true; // flag: memo miss
                }
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Control Flow ───────────────────────────────────────
            .JMP => {
                self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
            },
            .JZ => {
                if (self.state.regs.flags.zero) {
                    self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                } else {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                }
            },
            .JNZ => {
                if (!self.state.regs.flags.zero) {
                    self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                } else {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                }
            },
            .JN => {
                if (self.state.regs.flags.negative) {
                    self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                } else {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                }
            },
            .CALL => {
                // Push return address
                self.state.regs.sp -%= 8;
                const ret_addr: i64 = @intCast(self.state.regs.pc + 1);
                self.state.mem.write64(self.state.regs.sp, ret_addr) catch return error.StackOverflow;
                self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(instr.imm9);
            },
            .RET => {
                const ret_addr = self.state.mem.read64(self.state.regs.sp) catch return error.StackUnderflow;
                self.state.regs.sp +%= 8;
                self.state.regs.pc = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(ret_addr)));
            },
            .HALT => {
                self.state.regs.flags.halted = true;
                self.state.running = false;
            },
            .YIELD => {
                // Yield back to FFN for one cycle, resume next tap
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                self.state.running = false; // exits executeTap loop
            },
            .NOP => {
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Dream & Canvas ─────────────────────────────────────
            .DREAM => {
                self.state.enterDream(@intCast(instr.imm9));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .WAKE => {
                self.state.wake();
                self.state.running = false; // return to token emission
            },
            .DPIX => {
                const x: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                const y: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                const color_val: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                self.state.canvas.setPixel(x, y, @bitCast(color_val));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Meta / Self-Modification ───────────────────────────
            .EMIT => {
                if (!self.config.self_modify_enabled) {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                    return;
                }
                // Write instruction word from R[rs1] to program address R[rs2]
                const word: u32 = @intCast(@as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1))) & 0xFFFFFFFF);
                const addr = core.PROGRAM_BASE + @as(u64, @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs2))) * 4;
                const bytes: [4]u8 = @bitCast(word);
                for (bytes, 0..) |b, i| {
                    self.state.mem.write8(addr + i, b) catch return error.MemoryAccessViolation;
                }
                self.state.regs.flags.self_modify = true;
                self.state.total_fused_ops += 1;
                log.info("[axiNC] EMIT: wrote instruction 0x{X:0>8} at addr 0x{X:0>8}", .{ word, addr });
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .LEARN => {
                if (!self.config.self_modify_enabled) {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                    return;
                }
                // Store value in Tricache at SPZA-derived key
                const spza_idx: usize = @intCast(instr.rs1 & 0x7);
                const spza_reg = &self.state.regs.spza[spza_idx];
                const value = self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rd);
                const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(
                    @truncate(spza_reg.dims[0]),
                    @truncate(spza_reg.dims[1]),
                    0x4C524E, // "LRN"
                );
                self.axicore_ctx.cache.store(key, value, 0x4C524E);
                log.info("[axiNC] LEARN: cached value={d} at SPZA[{d}] → Tricache", .{ value, spza_idx });
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .FUSE => {
                if (!self.config.self_modify_enabled) {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                    return;
                }
                // Fuse: takes start_pc and length from registers,
                // reads that instruction sequence, registers as custom opcode
                const start: u64 = @bitCast(self.state.regs.getGP(instr.rs1));
                const len: u64 = @intCast(instr.imm9);
                if (len > isa.MAX_FUSED_SEQUENCE or len == 0) {
                    self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                    return;
                }
                var seq: [isa.MAX_FUSED_SEQUENCE]isa.Instruction = undefined;
                for (0..@intCast(len)) |i| {
                    const word = self.fetch(start + i) catch {
                        self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                        return;
                    };
                    seq[i] = isa.Instruction.decode(word);
                }
                const name = "FUSED"; // model can set name via LANG later
                if (self.custom_registry.register(name, seq[0..@intCast(len)])) |opcode_id| {
                    self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, @intCast(opcode_id));
                    self.state.custom_opcodes += 1;
                    self.state.total_fused_ops += 1;
                }
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            .LANG => {
                // LANG is the capstone: define a named opcode
                // For now, delegates to FUSE with a name from memory
                // Full implementation reads grammar from axiNC memory
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
                log.info("[axiNC] LANG: custom language definition (stub)", .{});
            },
            .INTRO => {
                // Introspection: read instruction at PC + offset
                const offset: i16 = instr.immSigned();
                const target_pc: u64 = @intCast(@as(i64, @intCast(self.state.regs.pc)) + offset);
                const word = self.fetch(target_pc) catch 0;
                self.state.regs.setGP(instr.rd, @intCast(word));
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
            // ── Catch-all ──────────────────────────────────────────
            .INVALID => return error.InvalidOpcode,
            else => {
                log.warn("[axiNC] unimplemented opcode 0x{X:0>2} at PC={d}", .{ instr.opcode, self.state.regs.pc });
                self.state.regs.pc += 1;
            },
        }
    }
    /// Execute a custom (LANG-defined) opcode by expanding its sequence
    fn executeCustom(self: *Engine, instr: isa.Instruction) !void {
        const slot = instr.customSlot() orelse return error.CustomOpcodeNotFound;
        const sequence = self.custom_registry.expand(slot) orelse return error.CustomOpcodeNotFound;
        // Execute each instruction in the fused sequence
        for (sequence) |sub_instr| {
            try self.execute(sub_instr);
        }
        // PC already advanced by sub-instructions
    }
    // ── Utility ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    /// Load a program (slice of instruction words) into memory
    pub fn loadProgram(self: *Engine, instructions: []const isa.Instruction) !void {
        var buf: [4096]u8 = undefined;
        var pos: usize = 0;
        for (instructions) |instr| {
            const word = instr.encode();
            const bytes: [4]u8 = @bitCast(word);
            @memcpy(buf[pos .. pos + 4], &bytes);
            pos += 4;
        }
        try self.state.mem.loadProgram(buf[0..pos]);
        self.state.regs.pc = 0;
        self.state.regs.sp = core.STACK_BASE;
        log.info("[axiNC] program loaded | {d} instructions", .{instructions.len});
    }
    /// Get execution statistics including axicore savings
    pub fn getStats(self: *const Engine) Stats {
        const cache_stats = self.axicore_ctx.cache.stats();
        const alu_report = self.scalar_alu.report();
        return .{
            .total_cycles = self.state.total_cycles,
            .total_instructions = self.state.total_instructions,
            .custom_opcodes = self.state.custom_opcodes,
            .total_fused_ops = self.state.total_fused_ops,
            // Tricache stats
            .tricache_l1_hit_rate = cache_stats.l1_hit_rate,
            .tricache_l2_hit_rate = cache_stats.l2_hit_rate,
            .tricache_l3_hit_rate = cache_stats.l3_hit_rate,
            .tricache_overall_hit_rate = cache_stats.overall_hit_rate,
            // ALU stats
            .alu_cache_hits = alu_report.cache_hits,
            .alu_shift_add_ops = alu_report.shift_add_computes,
            .alu_cache_hit_rate = alu_report.cache_hit_rate,
            // Energy
            .energy_saved = self.axicore_ctx.energy_saved_estimate,
            .hw_backend = self.axicore_ctx.hw.primary,
            .vram_usage_mb = self.state.vramUsageMB(),
            .dream_mode = self.state.dream_mode,
        };
    }
    pub const Stats = struct {
        total_cycles: u64,
        total_instructions: u64,
        custom_opcodes: u16,
        total_fused_ops: u64,
        // Tricache (L1/L2/L3) performance
        tricache_l1_hit_rate: f32,
        tricache_l2_hit_rate: f32,
        tricache_l3_hit_rate: f32,
        tricache_overall_hit_rate: f32,
        // ALU compute savings
        alu_cache_hits: u64,
        alu_shift_add_ops: u64,
        alu_cache_hit_rate: f32,
        // Energy and hardware
        energy_saved: u64,
        hw_backend: axicore.HwBackend,
        vram_usage_mb: usize,
        dream_mode: bool,
    };
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Tests
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
test "engine: simple add program" {
    var state = try core.MachineState.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer state.deinit(std.testing.allocator);
    var engine = try Engine.init(std.testing.allocator, &state, .{});
    defer engine.deinit();
    // Program: R0=7, R1=6, R2=R0+R1, HALT
    const program = [_]isa.Instruction{
        isa.Builder.movi(0, 7),
        isa.Builder.movi(1, 6),
        isa.Builder.add(2, 0, 1),
        isa.Builder.halt(),
    };
    try engine.loadProgram(&program);
    _ = try engine.executeTap();
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 13), state.regs.getGP(2));
    try std.testing.expect(state.regs.flags.halted);
}
test "engine: multiply with memoization" {
    var state = try core.MachineState.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer state.deinit(std.testing.allocator);
    var engine = try Engine.init(std.testing.allocator, &state, .{});
    defer engine.deinit();
    const program = [_]isa.Instruction{
        isa.Builder.movi(0, 7),
        isa.Builder.movi(1, 6),
        isa.Builder.mul(2, 0, 1), // 7 * 6 = 42
        isa.Builder.halt(),
    };
    try engine.loadProgram(&program);
    _ = try engine.executeTap();
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), state.regs.getGP(2));
}
test "engine: conditional jump" {
    var state = try core.MachineState.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer state.deinit(std.testing.allocator);
    var engine = try Engine.init(std.testing.allocator, &state, .{});
    defer engine.deinit();
    // Program: R0=5, R1=5, CMP R0,R1, JZ to addr 5, R2=99 (skip), R2=42, HALT
    const program = [_]isa.Instruction{
        isa.Builder.movi(0, 5), // 0
        isa.Builder.movi(1, 5), // 1
        isa.Builder.rrr(.CMP, 0, 0, 1), // 2: CMP R0, R1 → zero flag set
        isa.Builder.imm(.JZ, 5), // 3: JZ 5 → jump to MOVI R2,42
        isa.Builder.movi(2, 99), // 4: skipped
        isa.Builder.movi(2, 42), // 5: R2=42
        isa.Builder.halt(), // 6
    };
    try engine.loadProgram(&program);
    _ = try engine.executeTap();
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), state.regs.getGP(2));
}
test "engine: yield resumes" {
    var state = try core.MachineState.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer state.deinit(std.testing.allocator);
    var engine = try Engine.init(std.testing.allocator, &state, .{});
    defer engine.deinit();
    const program = [_]isa.Instruction{
        isa.Builder.movi(0, 10), // 0
        isa.Builder.yield_(), // 1: yield back to FFN
        isa.Builder.movi(1, 20), // 2: resumes here on next tap
        isa.Builder.halt(), // 3
    };
    try engine.loadProgram(&program);
    // First tap: executes MOVI R0,10 then YIELD
    _ = try engine.executeTap();
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 10), state.regs.getGP(0));
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 0), state.regs.getGP(1)); // not yet
    // Second tap: resumes at PC=2
    state.running = true;
    _ = try engine.executeTap();
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 20), state.regs.getGP(1)); // now set
}
 
---
// AxiMinds Neural Computer — ALU (Arithmetic Logic Unit)
// Implements all Tier 0 compute ops via axicore primitives:
// - Native GPU integer ops (ADD, SUB, AND, OR, XOR, shifts)
// - Shift-add decomposition for MUL (avoids expensive multiplier)
// - Memoization for repeated computations
// - SPZA angular distance for spatial ops
//
// Key difference from nCPU: we use ACTUAL arithmetic, not neural inference.
// nCPU: ADD R0,R1,R2 → 8 neural forward passes (~248µs)
// axiNC: ADD R0,R1,R2 → 1 native GPU instruction (~1ns)
const std = @import("std");
const core = @import("../core/types.zig");
const axicore = @import("../core/axicore.zig");
const isa = @import("../isa/opcodes.zig");
const log = std.log.scoped(.axinc_alu);
/// ALU result with flags and savings metadata
pub const AluResult = struct {
    value: i64,
    carry: bool = false,
    overflow: bool = false,
    cache_hit: bool = false, // served from Tricache (L1/L2/L3)?
    mep_path: axicore.MEP.Path = .shift_add, // which energy path was taken?
    energy_cost: u32 = 0, // relative compute energy spent
};
/// Vector ALU result
pub const VecResult = struct {
    values: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32,
    scalar: ?i64 = null, // for reduction ops (VDOT, VRED)
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Scalar ALU — Full axicore compute savings pipeline
//
// Every operation routes through:
// 1. Tricache L1→L2→L3 lookup (cheapest path)
// 2. On miss: ShiftAdd compute (zero hardware MUL)
// 3. INT1 consensus verify (for .verified precision)
// 4. Result stored back into Tricache (all tiers)
// 5. MEP tracks energy savings
//
// The AI's neural computer gets ALL of this, not a subset.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const ScalarAlu = struct {
    ctx: *axicore.AxicoreContext, // full axicore stack
    // Per-ALU statistics
    ops_executed: u64 = 0,
    cache_hits: u64 = 0,
    shift_add_computes: u64 = 0,
    energy_saved: u64 = 0,
    pub fn init(ctx: *axicore.AxicoreContext) ScalarAlu {
        return .{ .ctx = ctx };
    }
    /// ADD: Native addition with overflow detection
    /// ADD is already 1 cycle, no memoization needed (cheaper to compute than lookup)
    pub fn add(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const result = @addWithOverflow(a, b);
        return .{
            .value = result[0],
            .carry = result[1] != 0,
            .overflow = result[1] != 0,
            .mep_path = .shift_add,
            .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add),
        };
    }
    /// SUB: Native subtraction with borrow detection
    pub fn sub(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const result = @subWithOverflow(a, b);
        return .{
            .value = result[0],
            .carry = result[1] != 0,
            .overflow = result[1] != 0,
            .mep_path = .shift_add,
            .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add),
        };
    }
    /// MUL: Full axicore pipeline
    /// Tricache L1→L2→L3 → ShiftAdd → Tricache store
    /// Zero hardware multiplies. All energy tracked.
    pub fn mul(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        // Commutative key: canonical order for better cache hit rate
        const lo = @min(a, b);
        const hi = @max(a, b);
        const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(lo, hi, 0x4D554C);
        // Tricache hierarchical lookup
        if (self.ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.cache_hits += 1;
            self.ctx.total_cache_saves += 1;
            self.energy_saved += axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add);
            return .{
                .value = cached,
                .cache_hit = true,
                .mep_path = .cached,
                .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.cached),
            };
        }
        // Cache miss: shift-add compute (zero hardware MUL)
        const result = axicore.ShiftAdd.mul(a, b);
        self.shift_add_computes += 1;
        self.ctx.total_shift_add_ops += 1;
        // Store in all Tricache tiers
        self.ctx.cache.store(key, result, 0x4D554C);
        return .{
            .value = result,
            .mep_path = .shift_add,
            .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.shift_add),
        };
    }
    /// MUL with INT1 consensus verification (for critical paths)
    /// Computes via shift-add, verifies result with N-voter consensus
    pub fn mulVerified(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64, tier: axicore.Int1Consensus.Tier) AluResult {
        const result = self.mul(a, b);
        // Recompute independently for consensus
        const verify = axicore.ShiftAdd.mul(a, b);
        const consensus = axicore.Int1Consensus.verifyMemo(result.value, verify, tier);
        self.ctx.total_consensus_checks += 1;
        if (!consensus.result) {
            log.warn("[ALU] MUL consensus FAILED | a={d} b={d} got={d} verify={d} confidence={d:.3}", .{
                a, b, result.value, verify, consensus.confidence,
            });
            // Return recomputed value on consensus failure
            return .{
                .value = verify,
                .mep_path = .full,
                .energy_cost = axicore.MEP.energyCost(.full),
            };
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// DIV: Iterative shift-subtract division through Tricache
    pub fn div(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) !AluResult {
        if (b == 0) return error.DivisionByZero;
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(a, b, 0x444956); // "DIV"
        if (self.ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.cache_hits += 1;
            self.ctx.total_cache_saves += 1;
            return .{ .value = cached, .cache_hit = true, .mep_path = .cached };
        }
        // Shift-subtract binary long division
        const sign_a = a < 0;
        const sign_b = b < 0;
        const abs_a: u64 = if (sign_a) @intCast(-a) else @intCast(a);
        const abs_b: u64 = if (sign_b) @intCast(-b) else @intCast(b);
        var quotient: u64 = 0;
        var remainder: u64 = 0;
        for (0..64) |i| {
            const bit = 63 - i;
            remainder <<= 1;
            remainder |= (abs_a >> @intCast(bit)) & 1;
            if (remainder >= abs_b) {
                remainder -= abs_b;
                quotient |= @as(u64, 1) << @intCast(bit);
            }
        }
        const result_sign = sign_a != sign_b;
        const signed_result: i64 = if (result_sign)
            -@as(i64, @intCast(quotient))
        else
            @intCast(quotient);
        self.ctx.cache.store(key, signed_result, 0x444956);
        return .{ .value = signed_result, .mep_path = .shift_add };
    }
    /// MOD: Remainder after division, through Tricache
    pub fn mod(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) !AluResult {
        if (b == 0) return error.DivisionByZero;
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const key = axicore.ShiftAdd.computeKey(a, b, 0x4D4F44); // "MOD"
        if (self.ctx.cache.lookup(key)) |cached| {
            self.cache_hits += 1;
            return .{ .value = cached, .cache_hit = true, .mep_path = .cached };
        }
        const result = @rem(a, b);
        self.ctx.cache.store(key, result, 0x4D4F44);
        return .{ .value = result };
    }
    /// Bitwise AND (no cache needed, cheaper to compute)
    pub fn bitAnd(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a & b };
    }
    /// Bitwise OR
    pub fn bitOr(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a | b };
    }
    /// Bitwise XOR
    pub fn bitXor(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a ^ b };
    }
    /// Bitwise NOT
    pub fn bitNot(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = ~a };
    }
    /// Shift left
    pub fn shl(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, shift: u6) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const carry_bit = (a >> @as(u6, @intCast(@as(u7, 63) - @as(u7, shift)))) & 1 != 0;
        return .{ .value = a << shift, .carry = carry_bit };
    }
    /// Shift right (arithmetic)
    pub fn shr(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, shift: u6) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        return .{ .value = a >> shift };
    }
    /// Compare: subtraction without storing result, only flags
    pub fn cmp(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64, b: i64) AluResult {
        return self.sub(a, b);
    }
    /// Increment
    pub fn inc(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        return self.add(a, 1);
    }
    /// Decrement
    pub fn dec(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        return self.sub(a, 1);
    }
    /// Negate
    pub fn neg(self: *ScalarAlu, a: i64) AluResult {
        self.ops_executed += 1;
        const result = @subWithOverflow(@as(i64, 0), a);
        return .{ .value = result[0], .overflow = result[1] != 0 };
    }
    /// Get ALU performance report
    pub fn report(self: *const ScalarAlu) AluReport {
        const total = self.ops_executed;
        return .{
            .total_ops = total,
            .cache_hits = self.cache_hits,
            .shift_add_computes = self.shift_add_computes,
            .cache_hit_rate = if (total == 0) 0.0 else
                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.cache_hits)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(total)),
            .energy_saved = self.energy_saved,
        };
    }
    pub const AluReport = struct {
        total_ops: u64,
        cache_hits: u64,
        shift_add_computes: u64,
        cache_hit_rate: f32,
        energy_saved: u64,
    };
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Vector ALU — SIMD-width batch operations with axicore savings
// All multiplies route through ShiftAdd. Dot products use shift-add
// per element pair. Maps to NEON/AVX/CUDA warps via HwDispatch.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const VectorAlu = struct {
    /// Element-wise vector addition
    pub fn vadd(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        var result: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = undefined;
        for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
            result[i] = a[i] +% b[i]; // wrapping add for SIMD semantics
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// Element-wise vector subtraction
    pub fn vsub(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        var result: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = undefined;
        for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
            result[i] = a[i] -% b[i];
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// Element-wise vector multiply — ALL through ShiftAdd, zero hardware MUL
    pub fn vmul(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        var result: [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 = undefined;
        for (0..core.VEC_WIDTH) |i| {
            // Each element multiply is shift-add decomposed
            const product = axicore.ShiftAdd.mul(@intCast(a[i]), @intCast(b[i]));
            result[i] = @truncate(product);
        }
        return result;
    }
    /// Dot product: sum(a[i] * b[i]) → scalar i64
    /// Uses ShiftAdd.dotProduct for zero hardware multiplies
    pub fn vdot(a: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, b: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32) i64 {
        return axicore.ShiftAdd.dotProduct(a, b);
    }
    /// Reduction operations
    pub const ReduceOp = enum(u4) {
        sum = 0,
        max = 1,
        min = 2,
        avg = 3,
    };
    pub fn vred(v: *const [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32, op: ReduceOp) i64 {
        return switch (op) {
            .sum => blk: {
                var acc: i64 = 0;
                for (v) |elem| acc += @as(i64, elem);
                break :blk acc;
            },
            .max => blk: {
                var m: i32 = std.math.minInt(i32);
                for (v) |elem| m = @max(m, elem);
                break :blk @as(i64, m);
            },
            .min => blk: {
                var m: i32 = std.math.maxInt(i32);
                for (v) |elem| m = @min(m, elem);
                break :blk @as(i64, m);
            },
            .avg => blk: {
                var acc: i64 = 0;
                for (v) |elem| acc += @as(i64, elem);
                break :blk @divTrunc(acc, core.VEC_WIDTH);
            },
        };
    }
    /// Broadcast scalar to all vector lanes
    pub fn vsplat(scalar: i32) [core.VEC_WIDTH]i32 {
        return [_]i32{scalar} ** core.VEC_WIDTH;
    }
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// SPZA ALU — Spatial addressing operations
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pub const SpzaAlu = struct {
    /// Compute angular distance between two SPZA coordinates
    pub fn distance(a: *const core.SpzaCoord, b: *const core.SpzaCoord) u128 {
        return a.angularDistance(b);
    }
    /// Normalize SPZA coordinate to unit sphere at zNorm scale (2^70)
    pub fn normalize(coord: *core.SpzaCoord) void {
        // Compute magnitude via shift-add sqrt approximation
        var sum_sq: u256 = 0;
        inline for (0..8) |i| {
            const v: i256 = @intCast(coord.dims[i]);
            sum_sq += @as(u256, @intCast(if (v < 0) -v else v)) *
                @as(u256, @intCast(if (v < 0) -v else v));
        }
        // Newton-Raphson sqrt via shift-add (axicore style)
        if (sum_sq == 0) return;
        var mag: u256 = 1;
        // Rough initial estimate via leading bit
        var temp = sum_sq;
        var bits: u32 = 0;
        while (temp > 0) : (bits += 1) temp >>= 1;
        mag = @as(u256, 1) << @intCast(bits / 2);
        // 3 Newton iterations (sufficient for our precision)
        for (0..3) |_| {
            if (mag == 0) break;
            mag = (mag + sum_sq / mag) >> 1;
        }
        // Scale each dimension to zNorm (2^70)
        const z_norm: u256 = @as(u256, 1) << 70;
        if (mag == 0) return;
        inline for (0..8) |i| {
            const scaled: i256 = (@as(i256, @intCast(coord.dims[i])) * @as(i256, @intCast(z_norm))) /
                @as(i256, @intCast(mag));
            coord.dims[i] = @truncate(scaled);
        }
        coord.magnitude = @truncate(z_norm);
    }
};
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Tests
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
test "scalar ALU: add" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = alu.add(40, 2);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(!r.carry);
}
test "scalar ALU: shift-add mul" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = alu.mul(7, 6);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r.value);
}
test "scalar ALU: mul negative" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = alu.mul(-7, 6);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, -42), r.value);
}
test "scalar ALU: mul tricache hit" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    _ = alu.mul(123, 456); // first: compute via shift-add
    const r = alu.mul(123, 456); // second: Tricache L1 hit
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 56088), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(r.cache_hit);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(axicore.MEP.Path.cached, r.mep_path);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 1), alu.cache_hits);
}
test "scalar ALU: mul commutative cache" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    _ = alu.mul(7, 6); // store with canonical key min(7,6)=6, max=7
    const r = alu.mul(6, 7); // same canonical key: cache hit
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 42), r.value);
    try std.testing.expect(r.cache_hit);
}
test "scalar ALU: div" {
    var ctx = try axicore.AxicoreContext.init(std.testing.allocator);
    defer ctx.deinit();
    var alu = ScalarAlu.init(&ctx);
    const r = try alu.div(42, 6);
    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i64, 7), r.value);
}
test "scalar ALU: div by zero" {
